rje btsun 'jigs med 'phrin las rgya mtsho dpal bzang bo'i rnam  ku mA ra sU r+ya nA ma b+ha T+TA ka ra a b+h+ya karma sa par thar ba dad pa'i pad mo bzhad pa'i bden gtam nyi ma gzhon nu  ra shrI b+ha dra sya bya k+Sha raM bi ha ra ti sma / /
zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /

a trA saH da sha ba laH rA dzyAM si taM @# / /
'jigs med stobs bcu'i rgyal thabs la gnas shing /
ka rmA k+Shau hi Ni ba laM bi krA n+ta b+hiH /
'phrin las a k+Shau hi Ni'i dpung rtsal gyis /
pa ny+tsaM tI bru ru tsa laM sha trwaH ha taH lnga bdo'i smag chen dgra tshogs rab bcom ste /
prA bI snA tha ga ta sa b+hiH nA ya te / /
gdul bya rgya mtsho 'dren pa'i mgron des skyongs / /
'jigs med stobs bcu'i rgyal thabs la gnas shing / /
'phrin las a k+Shau hi Ni'i dpung rtsal gyis / /
lnga bdo'i smag chen dgra tshogs rab bcom ste / /
gdul bya rgya mtsho 'dren pa'i mgon des skyongs / /
thugs bskyed rgya mtsho bsrubs las legs 'khrungs sa bcu'i shar ri'i rtser 'phags te / /
gang 'dul sku yi gzugs brnyan bye ba chu klung 'bum du rab spros pa / /
bu ram shing ba zhes pa'i mtshan gyi bdud rtsis rgud pa kun sel pa'i / /
rnam 'dren bzhi ba shAkya seng+ge 'bral med gtsug gi rgyan du 'dzin / /
gang gi sang mdzod gser gyi 'khor lo sgyur mkhas pa / /
mchog zung 'od srung kun dga' bo dang nye bar 'khor / /
la sogs dgra bcom 'phags tshogs bka' drin ches lci ba / /
gser ldan sgeg mos theg 'di ngo mtshar rmad du byung / /
ded dpon mkhas pas gru rdzings legs bcas nas / /
bsam 'phel nor bu drangs pas rgud pa bsal / /
'jig rten mig gyur skad gnyis smra ba yis / /
mdo rgyud rin chen drangs pas rgud pa bsal / /
rgyal kun mkhyen rab dmar ser 'od du 'tsher ba'i nyi ma che / /
ngur smrig gar du rtsen pa'i ston mchog slar yang byon pa bzhin / /
rgyal bstan mtha' dag rmang nas gsos pas blo bzang rgyal ba zhes / /
grags pa'i sgra chen srid pa'i khongs las brgal ba gtsug tu bsten / /
de yi sras mchog skye 'gro'i gnyen dang rgud mun dgrar gyur pa / /
rgyal tshab dam pa dar ma rin chen mkhas grub dge legs dpal / /
la sogs mkhas grub brgyud par bcas pa'i zla bral 'phrin las la / /
rnam par dpyod pa'i blo gros ldan pa su zhig gus mi 'gyur / /
kun mkhyen 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa zhes grags mkhas dgu'i gtsug gi rgyan / /
'chad rtsod rtsom gyi 'od brgya 'bar bas rmongs pa'i smag chen bsal / /
thub bstan pad tshal bskyangs pas bde skyid sbrang rtsi'i dga' ston rgyas / /
rdzogs ldan gsar ba'i byed po de la bdag snying rab tu gus / /
de yi skyes rabs sku tshe 'phreng brgyud slob dang yang slob bcas / /
'chad rtsod rtsom pa'i dpal 'bar rgyu skar gangs la 'khu ba yi / /
mkhas dang grub pa'i dpal gyis thub bstan spel ba'i rnam par thar / /
ro 'dzin stong du sprul nas bskal brgyar brjod kyang zad mtha' bral / /
khyad par che rgu kun gyi gtsug gi nor / /
'jigs pa med pa'i 'phrin las 'od rlabs kyis / /
thub bstan po ba rnams kyi blor 'tsham zhing go sla ba /
gnas lnga rig pa'i snying bcud 'dus shing 'jug bde ba /
shes ldan rgan pas bklags na blo skyed gsar ba thob pa /
a gsar gzhon nus bklags na mos gus dbang med 'chor ba'i yon tan gyi mdzod chen po zhig yin pas /
rgya che'i klog pa po rnams kyi dge ba'i bshes dang brtse ba'i grogs su gyur cig gu / /
zhes 'di ga'i rtsom sgrig khang nas /
spyi lo zla tshes la phul /
sgrig pa po'i gtam /
slob dpon chen mo dmu dge bsam gtan rgya mtsho mchog ni /
deng dus bod mi rigs spyi'i gtsug tu mchod pa'i mkhas dbang chen po zhig red /
khong gis sku tshe gang bor rang mi rigs kyi rig gnas la thugs zhen zab bzhes ngos nyams pa sor chud /
ma nyams gong 'phel /
shes rig yar rgyas kyi don du brtse gzigs zol med /
brtson pa lhod med /
gsung dbyangs 'gag med kyis rang nus gang yod phul ba'i bka' drin ni bsam brjod yul las 'das pa zhig red /
lhag par du khong gis nga tshor bzhag pa'i rig gzhung gi shul bzhag rin po che la bltas kyin bltas kyin mos gus mchi ma rab tu 'khrigs /
bsam bzhin bsam bzhin rin thang gzhal du med pa shes /
nga rang tsho mi rigs dpe skrun gyi las ka byed mkhan zhig yin pa'i ngos nas bshad na /
slob dpon chen mo 'di ba'i phyag rtsom mtha' dag phyogs gcig tu bsdus te gsung 'bum cha tshang zhig bsgrigs nas par du bskrun na ni rang mi rigs kyi rig gnas bang mdzod la rin chen nor bu zhig bsnan pa lta bu'i dge mtshan chen po ldan zhing /
lar blo gsal gzhon nu'i tshogs la rig pa'i dngos po phun sum tshogs pa zhig mngon par bstabs pa'i phan yon shin tu mi dman pa zhig yod par mthong nas de lugs kyi brtson pa lhur len pa'i 'dun pa drag po snying la bcags khar /
nye lam rje nyid kyi sku sring bde mchog skyid dang khong gi yang tsha grwa btsun bslab gsum rgya mtsho zung gis sa thag ring bo'i dka' sdug la ma 'dzems par rje nyid kyi gsung rtsom mtha' dag dre'u khal du longs pa zhig dngos su khur nas rang re'i dpe skrun khang du slebs shing /
khyed dpe skrun khang gi rtsom sgrig spus tshad legs pas gzhan su dang gang la'ang ma sprad par khyed cag la gtad pa yin zhes gsung 'bum dpar skrun gyi dngos shugs dbang cha yod tshad nga tshor phul ba dang /
khyad par du nged dpe skrun khang la ma dngul gyi 'khos ka zhan pa mthong nas /
gcen po'i gsung 'bum par du btab nas bod mi rigs kyi rig gnas la phyar ba gru 'degs kyi nus pa thon na de las che ba med ces gsungs te gcen rin po che'i brtsams yon skar gcig kyang med pa'i thog da dung gzhan las zhal 'debs dngul sgor khri gnyis tsam bsdus nas gun gsab kyi rogs skyor byas pa la nga tsho sems 'gul chen po dang skul ma chen po thebs te /
gzhi nas khong gi gsung 'bum cha tshang zhig sgrig pa'i 'char gzhi dngos bstar byas pa yin /
da cha nga tshos par du bskrun pa'i gsung 'bum 'di la khyon bsdoms pod drug tu bkar /
pod dang po ni gtso cher rnam thar skor yin /
'di'i nang du nga tshos de snga sus kyang mjal ma myong ba'i mdo smad bstan pa'i bdag po rje bla kho rin po che 'jigs med 'phrin las rgya mtsho'i rnam thar lo rgyus mjal thub par ma zad /
rtsom pa po rang nyid kyi byung ba lo rgyus las mkhas chen dam pa zhig thos sbyang gi stobs ga 'dra zhig la brten nas 'tshar longs byung ba'i tshul la rgyus mnga' lon cing rang nyid la sbyang stobs che ru bskyed pa'i skul ma thebs nges yin /
pod gnyis pa ni gtso cher gzhung 'grel skor te /
'di'i nang nas rtsom pa po rang nyid nang don rig pa'i mkhas dbang zhig yin pa'i ngos nas deng gi 'chad grwa'i gzhung khrid kyi dka' gnad la dmigs nas tshig don gnyis gsal gyi 'grel bshad gnang yod /
pod gsum pa ni gtso cher lo rgyus skor te /
'di'i nang du bod kyi lo rgyus dang rig gnas dar tshul gyi lo rgyus sogs bkod yod pas /
nga tshos lo rgyus 'di dag las rtsom pa po'i lo rgyus zhib 'jug gi phul byung grub 'bras mthong thub par ma zad /
mkhas pa gzhan gyi gsung na med pa'i legs bshad btso ma'i gser lta bu'ang mi nyung ba zhig zin rgyu yod do / /
pod bzhi ba ni gtso cher sgra snyan ngag skar rtsis kyi skor yin /
'di'i nang du slob dpon 'di bas srol rgyun rig gnas kyi bslab bya so so rgyas bsdus 'tsham zhing go bde ba'i lam nas bkral yod pas las dang po ba rnams la nye bar mkho zhing 'jug bde ba'i gnas dam pa zhig tu 'khums so / /
pod lnga ba ni gtso cher sum rtags dag gsum skor yin /
'di'i nang nas nga tshos rtsom pa po'i deng rabs kyi khyad chos ldan pa'i brda sprod kyi gzhung lugs dang lta ba gsar ba /
lag len gyi rin thang ldan zhing nye bar mkho ba'i bshad pa gsar ba shes rtogs byed thub pa yin /
pod drug pa ni gsung thor bu'i skor te /
'di'i nang nas nga tshos rtsom pa pos gdul bya'i blo gang la gang 'tsham du sbyar ba'i shes bya sna tshogs /

mdor na /

rnam thar rtsom pa'i bya ba la zhugs so / /
de la 'dir mkhas dgu'i gtsug gi nor bu mdo sngags grub mtha' rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu phyin nas zab rgyas kyi gdams pa thugs nyams su bstar bas grub pa'i go 'phang mthon por slebs de snyigs ma'i dus 'dir sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa yongs su rdzogs pa'i srog 'dzin pa'i gsum ldan rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po mtshan brjod par dka' ba don gyi slad du mtshan nas smras na /

rnam 'dren bzhi ba shAkya seng+ge'i mdo sngags kyi bstan pa rin po che spel ba'i slad du 'phags pa'i yul dang gangs can gyi ljongs su sku'i skye ba bzhes pa'i 'khrungs rabs 'ga' zhig rje btsun bskal bzang thub bstan dbang phyug sogs ye shes kyi spyan ldan dag gis bka' lung 'khrul med las byung ba ni /

gzhan 'gyur gyi skye ba med pa stong nyid yin min dang /
yin na yongs grub kyi steng gi yin dgos la /
de lta na yongs grub stong gzhir byas te de chos gzhan gyis stong bas jo nang gi gzhan stong lta bur 'gyur ba dang /
bzod pa de kun re re la sbyor ba nyi shu re yod med sogs nya nyung mang po bsre ba byas zhes gsungs /
khong rang nyid kyis rnam thar sa bon shog dril skabs khengs skyungs sha stag gnang yang tshig don gnyis la byang chub nas sha zhag rus zhag tu song ba red /
de dag gi skabs su gtso bo rang gi yig cha bsdus grwa nas bzung ste thugs 'dzin gnang zhing tshogs rgyugs phul ba tsam du ma zad dpe khrid dang dpe gzigs don la zhib mor dpyad pa'i rgyu mtshan sogs kyis mkhas pa'i yang rtser son /
gung thang bstan pa'i sgron mes gsungs pa'i sgo mang chos dar ba'i rnam thar las /
deng sang slob gnyer la 'bad pa'i khul byed pa phal cher yang dpe char lta tshul rang gi yig cha 'dzin skyor byed rgyu bskyur nas dpe sna mang po zhig gis ma longs pa bzhin byas te dpe klog chab chob ra rtsi thog la yan pa bzhin thams cad kyi sne btog re byas rung gnad la 'bab rgyu gcig kyang med /
gzhung tshan de'i rang lugs bskyur te gzhan lugs pa'i dgag pa'i thad nas phar 'phen rgyu re e yod gtso bor byas pas skabs der 'gro thabs tsam 'ong yang /
rang la tshur 'phangs pa na 'bab sa 'di 'dra zhig dgos snyam du blor 'dzin rgyu'i gtad so zhig med stabs ri dwags thang la bdas pa bzhin gar 'gro 'dir 'gro med cing /
lo zla kha shas song dus sems ngo na ci yang med pa ni dang po slob gnyer rgyag dus rgyag ma shes pa'i skyon du snang ste kun mkhyen 'jigs med dbang po'i zhal snga nas /
gzhung tshig blo 'dzin mi byed gzhung gi don / /
dpe klog tsam gyis shes 'dod bzhad gad gnas / /
zhes dang /
thad ka'i gzhung la blta ba yal bor nas / /
dpe mang blta ba shes rab 'chal ba'i rgyu / /
gsungs pa ltar yin pas blo gsal ba rnams ya ma yeng gis nyi ma 'phul thabs de 'drar ma song bar dam pa 'di dag gi rnam thar la kha mig yar la blta ba zhig dgos so zhes gsungs pa ltar slob gnyer gsha' ma zhig byed 'dod pa dag gis bdag nyid chen po 'di'i rnam par thar ba ltar bslab par bya'o / /
gzhan yang mdo sde rgyan las /
rig pa'i gnas lnga dag la brtson par ma byas na / /
'phags mchog gis kyang thams cad mkhyen pa thob mi 'gyur / /
de bas gzhan dag tshar bcad rjes su bzung phyir dang / /

ces gsungs pa ltar 'phags chen dag gis gzhan don byed pa la med mi rung ba'i rig pa'i gnas la sbyangs shing mkhas par gyur pa yin te sngon gzhon nu'i dus stag ge dpon slob las sum rtags bslab cing /
'bro r+wa'i rgya mtsho'i drung nas skar rtsis kyi lnga bsdus nas bzung ste zhag gsum par ri mo rdzogs par sbyangs /
de rjes gso rig smra ba'i khyu mchog sman pa'i dung phrug zhes grags pa'i lnga rig pa 'jam dbyangs chos dar gyi zhal snga las dbyangs can sgra mdo rtsa 'grel gyi steng nas de dus sgra ba rnams la go tshor med pa'i gzhung gi bar bar gyi ri mo sgrub tshul lo chen thugs rje dpal dang /
a kyA yongs 'dzin gyi gsung du gsal ba de dang /
de dag tu mi gsal ba sngon gyi khrid rgyun du bzhugs pa dag dang bcas mdzub khrid lung bcas gsan sbyangs dang /
sdeb sbyor rin chen 'byung gnas rtsa 'grel mdzub khrid lung bcas nyan /
brda sprod kun bshad kyi mtshams su sleb pa na brda sprod mkhas pa dag gi mdzad srol bzhin brda sprod kun bshad kyi mtshan gsol /
slob dpon mchog de nyid kyis 'phags ma'i bstod pa dang 'dod don la smon pa'i gsol 'debs sngon du btang ste /

ma nor lam ston dran dbang tshul bzung ba / /

paN chen rjes su 'byor ba dang mtshungs pa / /
khyod mtshan dbyangs can dgyes pa'i rdo rje'o / /
zhes legs par sbyar ba saM skr-i ta'i skad dang shan sbyar yi ge dgu pa'i prA stA ras bcings pa bstsal te kun bshad kyi ming btags nas me tog 'thor ba dang bcas shis pa brjod pa'i mtha' brgyan to / /

khong mu to grags pa rgya mtsho las snyan ngag gsan /
snyan ngag la shin tu mkhas par gyur pa gsung rtsom rnams la bltas pa tsam gyis shes nus pa dper na don rgyan so lnga'i sgo nas 'jam pa'i dbyangs la bstod pa'i snyan ngag gsung 'bum khrod du bzhugs pa de lta bu'o / /
nag rtsis kyang nag rtsis sngon 'gro dang /

smras pa /
sngon gyi thugs bskyed sa bon grung bo las / /
nyer 'khrungs skyes sbyangs dpag bsam ljon pa'i rtser / /
lung rtogs me tog 'bum gyi rtse dga' ngom / /
dge mtshan dri bsung mngar bos 'jig rten khyab / /
'bad brtson skya rengs gsar bas nyer drangs pa'i / /
rnam dpyod nyi mas rang zhal ngom pa na / /
gzur gnas mtsho skyes 'bum gyi 'dab bzhad de / /
bstod bsngags b+h+ra ma ra yi glu dbyangs snyan / /
nyin mo'i mgon gyis rang 'od spros pa na / /
srid bya mun par thim pas 'khun sgra sgrog /
dam pa'i thos bsam 'od stong 'bar ba na / /
phrag dog khung bur nyal bas ngu co sgrog /
lho skya gos hrul thos dang tshul khrims kyis / /
thugs rgyud gser gyi bum bzang yongs su gtams / /
rigs lam zho 'thung rus pa'i rtse brgya yis / /
log rtog bcud med bdag po sde bcas bcom / /
zhes bla go rdo rje 'chang zhes yongs su grags pa rje btsun 'jigs med 'phrin las rgya mtsho dpal bzang bo'i rnam par thar ba dad pa'i padmo bzhad pa'i bden gtam nyi ma gzhon nu zhes bya ba las dang bor rgya chen thos pa mang du btsal ba'i sarga ste dang bo'o / /
bar du gzhung lugs thams cad gdams par shar ba'i sarga /
'jigs med mkhyen pa'i dkyil 'khor yongs su rdzogs / /
'phrin las 'od brgya 'bar ba'i 'od rlabs kyis / /
thub bstan rgya mtsho spel ba'i gnyen gcig pu / /
smra ba'i zla ba chen po rnam par rgyal / /
ded dpon mkhas pas yid bzhin dbang rgyal dang / /
mdzes ldan 'ching bu'i khyad par 'byed pa ltar / /
mnog chung srid pa'i nor dang thar ba'i bde / /
rnam par 'byed pa'i tshul de rmad du byung / /
bar du gzhung lugs thams cad gdams par shar ba'i tshul bshad pa la /
thog mar be'u bum sngon po las /
man ngag thams cad bsdus pa'i mgo ni / /
bshes gnyen dam pa mi btang ba yin / /
de las dad dang byang chub sems sogs / /
yon tan kun 'byung kun gyi gter yin / /
zhes dang /
rje thams cad mkhyen pas /
de nas 'di phyi'i legs tshogs ji snyed pa'i / /
rten 'brel legs par 'grig pa'i rtsa ba ni / /
lam ston bshes gnyen dam pa 'bad pa yis / /
bsam dang sbyor ba'i tshul bzhin bsten pa ru / /
mthong nas srog gi phyir yang mi gtong bar / /
bka' bzhin bsgrub pa'i mchod pas mnyes par byas / /
rnal 'byor ngas kyang nyams len de ltar byas / /
thar 'dod khyed kyang de bzhin skyangs 'tshal lo / /
zhes dang /
yon tan rin po che sdud pa las kyang /
slob ma bzang bo bla mar gus ldan de dag gis / /
bla ma mkhas pa rnams la rtag tu bsten par bya / /
ci phyir zhe na mkhas pa'i yon tan de las 'byung / /
zhes gsungs pa ltar phun sum tshogs pa thams cad kyi gzhi rten /
legs tshogs ma lus pa'i 'byung gnas /
mchog dang thun mong gi dngos grub thams cad kyi rtsa ba ni rnag la lam phyin ci ma log par ston pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen tshul bzhin tu bsten pa la rag las par gsungs pas so snyam du dge ba'i bshes gnyen gang bsten la dam tshig gi sel cung zad tsam yang ma song bar ma zad /
sangs rgyas dngos kyi 'du shes bzhag ste bsam sbyor gnyis kyis tshul bzhin du bsten pa dang /
khyad par bka' drin rjes su dran te gus par byas shing bka' bzhin bsgrub pa'i mchod pas mnyes par byas pa'i tshul ni /
khong stag ge tshang las klog bslabs pa dang sum rtags bslabs pas zhal nas khong bka' drin can des ka kha phral klog bslabs /
sbyar klog gzhal zhes pa'i bar bslabs te gzhan tsho bslab na zhar la shes yong 'gro gsungs nas skyabs 'gro ltung bshags sogs rim par bslabs pas bka' drin che zhes yang yang gsungs shing phyag thal mo sbyor /
deng sang chos par rlom pa 'gas klog slob pa'i slob dpon slob dpon du mi brtsi ba sogs la bltas na 'di ni gzhung lugs gdams par shar nas chos kyi gnad mkhyen pa'i rtags so / /
gzhan yang stag ge tshang gis khyod tshogs chos 'grim pa sogs la khang mig chung ngu zhig gis chog gsungs pa dang du blangs pa sogs gang gsungs bka' bzhin bsgrubs /
mkhan rin po che ngag dbang thub bstan rgya mtsho tshul bzhin bsten nas dbang bka' mang bo gsan zhing bka' bzhin bsgrubs pas thugs shin tu mnyes shing khong gi gsung las pha nor bu la bstsal ba bzhin ci tsam pa'i bka' dam po zhig la'ang dbang gral nas phud ma myong zhing khyad par 'jigs byed dmar po mda' 'gengs kyi dug dbang skabs ched gnyer gyis 'bod mi btang ba sogs thugs kyis rjes su bzung ba tshad med /
lhag par grub dbang yongs kyi 'khor los bsgyur ba lo hu ba'i lugs kyi dpal 'khor lo bde mchog lha re gnyis kyi dkyil 'khor du thog mar smin par mdzad pa'i bka' drin sogs bskal ba bye bar lus srog longs spyod kyis mchod kyang gzhal dka' ba'i drin chen po yin lags zhes shog dril la bris nas bzhag a khu rin po che rje zhang ston bstan pa rgya mtsho bsten nas gsung rtsom 'bri ba sogs phyag g.yog bsnyen bkur dang bka' bzhin bsgrub pa'i mnyes par byas pas thugs zin gyi slob mar gyur te khyod nged kyi rtsar 'di zhig tu bzung ste rgyud par lo shas 'gror bcug pa snyam pa yod mod ces gsungs pa dang /
bla go rdo rje 'chang khong gis rgyud du po to ba chen po'i zhal nas /
bsre bslad mi bya 'brel mi bya / /
ltogs 'jen mi bya 'dris mi bya / /
gyong du bya zhing 'grog dka' bya / /
zhes gsungs pa ltar /
'jig rten pa dag dang mi mthun zhing 'grog dka' ba byas nas bsgrub pa 'ba' zhig la gzhol skabs shig khong a khu rin po che de nyid kyi zhal nas /
mi dang ma 'grog par 'dug mi thub /
su dang 'grog kyang skyon ye med pa zhig gtan mi srid /
mi dang 'grig rgyu gal che /
cung zad re la bsnyad btags nas spo langs kyin ma bsdad na bzang /
res gcig gnyis re la bsran btsugs te bsdad na spangs pa min yang mi mngon pa zhig tu 'gro rgyu yod /
kha ton mag mug gcig 'don rgyu las dpe char blta ba gtso bor gyis /
dpe char blta ba la tshogs bsags sgrib sbyong thams cad kyi gnad 'dug pas gal chen gyis zhes sogs mtshang la rgol ba'i bslab ston gnang ba la /
deng dus kyi slob ma zhig yin tshe spo ma langs kyang bden kha rang gis bzung nas bla ma'i gsung rna rgyab kyi ser bur byed pa las med mod /
khong rin po che 'di ba'i zhal nas /
mtshang la rgol ba'i bslab ston bka' drin du bstsal ba ni bskal ba bye ba'i bar du mgo la thod bzhin bkur te lus dang longs spyod kyis mchod kyang gzhal bar dka' ba'i bka' drin du 'khums zhes gsungs /
ha cang thugs zin gyi slob mar gyur stabs /
zhu ba po med kyang dbu ma'i rnam bshad dgongs pa rab gsal gyi bshad lung gnang nas zin bris kyis gsung stabs zin bris byas pa gzigs 'bul zhus par spyi khog bzang ste gang bshad ma thon 'dug mjug gi chos skyong skabs mgon po chos rgyal bsten dgos tshul bshad pa'i skabs kyi bshad pa 'di la don bsdu lta bu zhig las med /
zin bris kyi rigs 'di rang gis ngos zin pa dang sla chos 'dra ba yin yang gsung ris sor bzhag bkod na phyis go ba bskyed tshul 'dra min yong ba dang /
byin rlabs kyi khyad che ba yod ces gsungs pa sogs dang /
nyin gcig shog dril zhig gi dbu na /
tshad mar gyur pa 'gro la phan bzhed pa / /
ston pa bde gshegs skyobs pa tsong kha ba / /
sgo gsum gus pa chen pos phyag bgyid na / /
pha rjes bu yis zin par byin gyis rlobs / /
zhes bris pa zhig gnang ste 'di'i 'phro la mar bstod 'grel chen mo nas don ldan ma'i 'bru 'brel rnams rje nyid kyi gsung gtsang ma sor bzhag tu 'khod la shog gsungs pa ltar bris te phul bar /
'di ngas bskul ba yin rgyu byas te khyod kyi rtsom gyi thog mar zhog gsungs kyang /
rje btsun gyis /
cha lugs ha cang ngan na gshis kyi brnyas / /
gsungs pa bzhin gzan sham sogs 'phyor bo med /
go sa snyan grags ni med /
yon tan can gyi grags skam zhig kyang med pas kun gyis 'phya ba las mi 'ongs snyam sbyar byang ma bzhag par phul ba bzhin nyid nas gsung 'bum khrod de bzhin bzhag 'dug ces gsungs /
'di yang bla ma'i thugs zin pa'i rnam thar rlabs po che'o / /
yang zhal nas nga rgyal ma chen bzang sogs skabs skabs kyi skyon gang shugs che na de nyid 'bur 'joms kyi bslab ston zhal ta rus pa can stsol ba sogs ma mdzangs kyis bu la bzhin lugs gnyis char nas bskyangs pa'i bka' drin bsam mtha' med mod ces gsungs pa sogs bka' drin rjes su dran pa'i rnam par thar ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o / /
yang khyod la mi ston na su la ston gsungs nas khams gsum rnam rgyal gyi dpe sprad pa dang /
dpe ris sogs 'brir bcug pa dang /
lam rim gyi bshad lung gi bar mtshams rnams su zhal khrus phul ba dang /
sku khams cung lci bar song ba'i skabs mtshams khong nas rnam rgyal gzungs ring dang /
'dus pa'i lus dkyil gyi sgo nas sum+b+ha ra dza sogs ci lcogs bsgrubs pas thugs zin /
nyin shas mtshams nas sku'i bab rgyun ldan dang /
gsung gleng rgyun chags phebs te /
pha ming bu la btags pa'i bla go tshang / /
snga ming phyi mar btags pa'i bla go tshang / /
da lta'i dus kyi phung gsum tsam po tshang / /
khyod la bze re can gyis 'di skad zhu / /
sogs ku re'i tshul du gsung 'phros kyi yi ge yang yang phebs pa sogs da lta dran pas mchi ma dku zhes gsungs pa yang bka' drin rjes su dran pa'i rnam thar ro / /
gzhan yang sku 'da' kha'i bar nyin re bzhin song ste stobs chen shugs bzlog dang zhal 'don gyi dgu gtor sogs btang zhes dang lung rtogs sku gshegs nged gnyis su khom gyis sku mdun du lam rim che ba dang legs bshad snying bo gnyis long skabs dang bstun shog byang 'ga' re snyan 'bul zhu bzhin yod ces dang /
bco lnga'i nyin khong gi zhabs rim du bzang spyod 'chi bslu zhig bton pa zhabs brtan phul ba'i tha ma yin zhes dang /
sku 'das rjes gdung mdun nas bde gsang 'jigs gsum gyi bdag 'jug dang /
tshe rabs kun du 'bral med rjes 'dzin gyi smon pa shugs drag dang /
gdung g.yog sogs las shor med pa zhus pas phyi nas sgo mang rin po che nas /
khyod kyis tshe 'dir go zhig chod pa de yin gsungs /
zhes sogs gsungs pa ni bshes gnyen tshul bzhin bsten pa'i rnam thar bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang rmad du byung ba yin te /
sngon 'brom ston pas jo bo chen po la ngas tshe stod chos byas pa gang lam du song zhus par /
jo bo'i zhal nas /
khyod kyis bla ma se btsun la g.yog byas pa de chos su song /
gzhan ma song gsungs pa ltar ro / /
gzhan yang skyabs mgon sku phreng bzhi ba bsam dang sbyor bas tshul bzhin bsten pa yin te /
ri khrod gong dge 'phel ri khrod du bzhugs skabs skyabs mgon mchog khong gi gzim shag chung ngur rgyun du phebs te gsung sgros dang zhal slob sogs kyis bslab ston dang lung bstan du ma gnang ba dang bka' dog pa'i zab chos du ma chig brgyud du bstsal ba sogs kyis rjes su bzung ba ma zad snang tshod la'ang thugs snang shin tu 'dris pa'i rnam pa bstan to / /
dper na khong gi gsung rnam thar sa bon las /
phyi nas skyabs mgon mchog spyil bur byon nas / /
ka ma la dang zla ba'i dkyil 'khor steng / /
zhes pa'i dbu can gyi sgrol dkar bstod pa zhig ljags rtsom gnang bar bskul ba po khyod yin rgyu byas zhes ri khrod kyi tshogs su btsugs /
ma 'gyang bar sgrol dkar bsnyen pa zhig gyis zhes phebs pas sgom khang gong nas sgrol dkar gyi bsnyen pa byas /
grub 'phral ri khrod du slebs pa na shul du nged kyi steng nas zing cha che tsam zhig bslangs 'dug kyang de ma thag mtshams bsdams nas chos rgyal gyi bsnyen pa zhig btang /
de grol du gong sa mchog gi byin gyis zing cha rang yal du song 'dug tshe'i bar chad cig yod pa bla ma dang 'phags ma'i byin rlabs kyis nyer 'tshe phra mo de tsam gyis bzlog pa yin mchi snyam du dad pa kha zhe med pa zhig skyes zhes gsungs pa ltar red /
de skabs dge 'dun rgya mtsho'i gsung las /
gcong rong nags kyi khrod na nyi ma bas / /
me khyer mchog tu rlom pa mthong bas skyo / /
zhes gsungs pa ltar /
ri khrod pa 'ga' zhig gis bshes gnyen nyi ma lta bu 'di'i yon tan mi mthong bar khong sgom khang gong du mtshams la bzhugs pa'i skabs /
ja sus thug sus skyel mi thub ces sogs kyi gleng brjod bslangs pa dang /
mthar gong sa skyabs mgon mchog la zhu rgyu byung tshe /
skyabs mgon mchog gi zhal nas /
khyod tsho'i ja sus thug sus de 'dra rtsa chen po zhig e red /
ngas 'di ba dgon pa zhig gi khri bar yang mngags ma bra bar bskyur yod pa 'di stong phrag gsum 'di la re rgyu zhig yod rgyu red snyam yod /
ces gsungs /
'di dus dgung lo nyer bzhi'i thog yin mod /
phyis su stong phrag gsum ma zad bod gangs can gyi sangs rgyas bstan pa'i srog 'dzin pa'i lung bstan yin no / /
yang khong gi zhal nas /
chos kyi bka' drin dang tha na sos bde gu yangs su tshe gang bor 'dug rgyu byung ba tshun gang gi bka' drin yin pas drin lan gzhal dka' bar yod /
ces sogs yang yang gsungs /
de ltar bsam pa dang sgrub pa'i mchod pas mnyes par byas pa ma zad /
bkur sti dang sbyor ba'i bsten tshul la yang shin tu zab par snang ste /
dper na skyabs mgon ri khrod du yun ring bzhugs skabs mchod gtor bzo bsham sogs mchod dpon gyi las gang dgos dang /
skyed ma ma 'tsho ba'i skabs kyang skar bcos dang /
khrus chog gang cir thugs bzhed ltar bsgrubs pa dang /
mi la'i rnam mgur 'don pa sogs phyag g.yog pher bo zhus zhes zhal nas gsungs /
gzhan yang de ltar bshes gnyen bsten tshul shin tu legs pa'i dbang gis bstan pa'i bdag por mnga' gsol ba yin te /
gzhan gyis bka' 'gyur gyi lung zhus par skyabs mgon dang sgo mang rin po cher bka' bgros byas par sgo mang rin po che'i zhal nas /
ngas thob kyang ma thob /
thob kyang 'don mi nus khyod kyis thon dang legs zhes gnang ba ltar bla grwa brgya lhag la bka' 'gyur gyi lung gnang /
de'i skabs shig skyabs mgon rdo rje 'chang nas bla brang sku tshab ched mngags kyis kha dar che legs shig bskur gnang mdzad de rje 'di bar /
gzhung bar lo bstar chags su lam rim bde lam dang 'jam dpal zhal lung gi khrid res mos su yod pa mi nub par skyong dgos zhes gsungs /
skabs der brel dbang gis dang len byed rgyu ma byung /
bka' 'gyur lung gnang tshar nas sku mdun du mjal bar 'phros mol zhib rgyas zhus par /
skyabs mgon rin po che'i zhal nas /
sngon chad dus skabs legs dus mnyam med sgrub khang ba /
dpon slob byams pa /
zhog don yod mkhas grub /
yongs 'dzin rin po che sogs kyis bde lam dang 'jam dpal zhal lung res mos kyis ston dpyid zla chos re gnang ba'i srol mchis /
da cha bod yul chos kyi zhing sar yang ming tsam yang dkon pa 'di red pas dgon sde 'di tsho bstan pa'i 'byung gnas gnyis par byed dgos rgyur 'dug pas res mos kyis lo re bzhin ma chad na legs snyam pa yin gsungs par /
rje 'di bas lags ji srid 'tsho'i bar nyid kyi dgongs bzhed ltar bsgrub ces zhus /
'di dag gis nang thugs kyi sras su gyur te chos kyi rgyal tshab tu dbang bskur ba shes sla'o / /
de bzhin du sgo mang rin po che blo bzang tshul khrims rgya mtsho dpal bzang bo yang bsam sbyor gnyis kyi sgo nas tshul bzhin bsten te zab pa dang rgya che ba'i chos bka' shin tu mang bo gsan /
khong gis chos mang bo gnang nas bstan pa'i bdag por dbang bskur bar dgongs te /
dbal mang tshang la gsung 'bum mang bo'i lung yod ces yang yang gsungs par brten dbal mang rin po che 'jam dbyangs bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho las gsung 'bum mang po dang gzhan dbang lung mang po zhus nas thob la chos bka' dkon pa mang bo zhig thob pas bka' drin che zhes bris 'dug pa dang /
rdo rje 'phreng ba'i dbang gnang skabs kyang de bzhin gsungs /
bka' 'gyur gyi lung gi skabs sgo mang rin po ches dpa' ris bstan 'dzin 'phrin las ched mngags kyis kha dar dkar ser che legs srid du ring ba zhig bskur te bka' 'gyur gyi 'chad nyan la thugs dgyes par yod tshul dang de bzhin phyis su'ang bka' chos 'chad spel rgya cher gnang dgos tshul sogs nang nyams dang sbyar ba'i blab bya mang du gnang ba sogs ni bstan pa'i bdag por mnga' gsol ba'o / /
'jam pa'i dbyangs gung thang rin po che bstan pa'i nyi ma las sngar gzhon dus nas chos bka' mang po gsan zhing phyis su'ang mang po gsan pa dang /
a mchog rin po che sogs chos 'brel gang thob la bka' drin dran pa'i dad gus tshad med pa mdzad /
'jam dbyangs chos dar ba'i zhal snga nas las sgra dang sdeb sbyor gsan skabs /
sngon nas 'brel ba'i mtshams sbyor zhig gis sam rje de nyid la skyon rtog skad cig kyang ma shar gsungs /
gzhan yang paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa sku gong ma dang phan tshun bla slob tu gyur /
khong gis zhal nas /
thams cad mkhyen gzigs mchog gis dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor zhal phyes te dbang bskur bzhes pas gsang sngags zab mo'i byin rlabs dang 'brel rlabs chen thugs bskyed smon pa'i rgya mtsho dang gcig tu lad mo tsam yin yang nan tan gyis byed bcug pa rgyal bstan spyi dang khyad par 'jam mgon ring lugs dar rgyas yun ring gi ched yin nges la zhar la mtha' med ngan song gi gting rdo bdag 'khor ba mtha' can du bsgrubs pa red snyam dga' dad shin tu rgyas shing nam dran res kyis kyang byung /
bka' drin de nyid stong gsum gser gyis bkang nas phul yang gzhal nus min zhes gsungs /
de ltar chos 'brel gang thob la dag snang tshad med pa mdzad pa sogs bshes gnyen bsten tshul legs pa'i rmang gzhi yod pa'i stobs kyis sku tshe ring zhing mdzad 'phrin phyogs med du rgyas /
snyigs dus 'dir bstan pa'i srog bzung zhing 'phrin las mkha' khyab tu rgyas pa'i 'bras rtags kyis bshes gnyen gang bsten la dam tshig gi sel ma zhugs shing bsten tshul ma log par grub bo / /
'on kyang zhi ba lhas /
mtho la phrag dog mnyam dang 'gran / /
dman la nga rgyal bstod na dregs / /
zhes pa'i mtshan nyid tshang ba re gnyis res log par rtog pa'i 'bras bu myong ste khyi rgan ku co che ba rang phung ber ka'i char 'bod du song bar ma zad rang rang mtha' rdugs su gyur pa mngon sum mo / /
gzhan yang gzhung lugs gdams par shar bas 'khor ba spyi bye brag las nges 'byung byang chub kyi sems rin po che la nges pa rnyed tshul ni /
sngar dpon tshang sogs kyis tsha kwan be shing gi khrir 'gro rgyu'i gros mgo bton pa thos 'phral thugs la shar ba gsungs tshul ni /
dpe shog ldeb gsum tsam yang 'dzin skyor yid phebs pa zhig mi 'byung zhes dang /
gzhung lugs la sbyangs pa'i skal ba lta ci kha ton mag mug re byed rgyu'i bsod nams yang mi 'dug pa ngo shes /
bde gsang sogs lhag lha 'di rnams la mtshams bsnyen sgrub re byed rgyu ma byung na de bas phung tshab che ba mi 'dug snyam yid mi bde /
zhes gsungs /
phyis su bshol thabs kyis phebs ma dgos pa 'dra /
'di ni rje'i byams bstod las /
bde med sdug bsngal brgya yis gtses pa yi / /
'khor ba'i phun tshogs yid la dran tsam gyis / /
lcags khang 'bar ba'i nang du tshud pa ltar / /
yid la 'dod pa til tsam med par shog /
ces gsungs pa ltar 'khor bde la zhen pa gting nas log pa'i rtags yin te /
bla sprul 'ga' zhig ltar khri kha gdan kha re e thob snyam du ang nyan byed pa ma yin par byang ba'i byis pa nyung mas mi mgu pa'i dpe ltar ro / /
yang zhal nas /
sngar nas bla ma nang chen gyi 'dzin bdag la zhe sun pa dang /
khong ri khrod pa tsho rje bstan pa'i sgron mes /
zhe sa ngo 'dzin dgos pa'i dpon po yang med cing / /
ze ba yar 'then dgos pa'i g.yog po yang med la / /
e gnod dogs pa dgos pa'i dgra bo yang med par / /
ye shes lha tshogs kho na bsten pa zhig byung na / /
zhes pa ltar skyid du tshor ba yod pa zhig mthong bas rang yang de 'dra zhig byung na snyam pa las 'char rgyu med ces gsungs /
dgung lo nyer lnga'i thog thar ba rtser phebs nas bsnyen mtshams shig gnang skabs /
srod thun la rkyen med par gting nas ngu snying zhig 'ongs nas mang po ngus zhes gsungs kyang rkyen med pa min te ma rgan sems can rnams sdug bsngal gyis mnar ba la mi bzod pa'i snying rje skyes pa'i rkyen gyis bshums pa dngul chu thogs med kyi rnam thar ltar yin te gsang rnam las /
rgyal yum rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i / /
zab lam rdo rje'i rnal 'byor rjes bskyangs pas / /
'gro la byams dang snying rje shugs drag gis / /
dbang med spyan chab chu bo'i rgyun bzhin babs / /
zhes gsungs pa ltar ro / /
de ltar gsung rab mtha' dag gi dgongs pa mthar thug ni gdul bya sems can mtha' dag 'khor ba phra rags kyi rgya mtsho las sgrol ched yin par dgongs shing /
gzhan dag 'khor ba phra rags las sgrol ba la sa lam gyi rim pa bgrod dgos /
de'i rtsa ba bshes gnyen dam pa tshul bzhin du bsten dgos pa yin la /

spyan ras gzigs kyi sku'i rnam pa yi ge phyed dang bzhi ba bya ba zhig yod pa de dang mthun /

yang khong gis gsungs pa /

da dung steng du song dang je gsal du 'gro zhes nan che ba byas kyang yom yom g.yo bas 'gro ma nus par ri'i phag na rgyal sras sku mched gsum bzhugs pa mjal du phyin /

po to ba dang yang mjal /

gang snang lha skur 'char ba'i rtogs pa brnyes pa dang /
yang mtshan lam du mkha' 'od dwangs gsal gyi rang bzhin na lha dang lha mo 'phan dang rgyal mtshan thogs pa mang po shar phyogs su 'gro ba'i rjes na lab lung skyabs mgon red zer ba'i 'ja' 'od kyi rang bzhin dwangs gsal sgrib med la sku mdangs smug po gdong zor ba /

de gnas byin rlabs che nges su 'dug ces gsungs pa yang brag dkar de 'khor lo bde mchog gi gnas yin pas bde mchog gi zhal gzigs par mngon mod zur tsam las mi gsungs 'dug rjes sor shel dgon du bzhugs skabs nam gung ma lon tsam na gam 'khod grwa chung zhig ra bar phyin pas gnas ri'i rtse nas 'ja' tshon nyis rim zhig shar ba'i sne khong bzhugs gnas kyi gzims khang steng du zug pa mthong pa bzhin ri khrod pa rnams kyis kyang mthong /

slar yang bdun thang gcig rnams bsdoms pas tshar bzhi /
rdo rje sems dpa' dang /
'jam dbyangs kyi thang ga che ba /
sman bla'i zhing bkod khyad mtshar te gsum po de ka'i sman pa'i 'du khang du bzhugs /
rdo rje mi 'khrugs pa'i thang ga che legs de ka'i ri khrod du bzhugs /
rje rin po che tsong kha brgyad cu'i zhal thang bco lnga gong bsham zhal kheb sogs bsdoms pas dngul rdo tshad re re song pa 'di bla brang tshogs chen 'du khang du bzhugs /
yang rje tsong kha brgyad cu gong gsham zhal kheb spus legs can gyi thang ga bco lnga sman pa'i 'du khang du bzhugs /
rdo rje mi 'khrugs pa'i gser sku che legs shig kyang der bzhag phyag rdor 'khor chen gyi thang sku che legs gcig bla brang rgyud khang du bzhag tshe lha rnam gsum rang gi lus tshad dang mnyam pa'i thang ga che ba gsum /
yang de 'dra'i tshe dpag med gcig ste bzhi /
rgyan drug mchog gnyis /
rta mgrin /
tshe dpag med /
dga' ldan lha brgya ma sogs bsdoms pas thang ga che chung sum cur nye ba hor tshang dgon gsar du bzhag yang dgon der 'od dpag med kyi zhing bkod gyan thang spus legs gcig bzhag sku phyogs 'khrungs rabs sogs thang ga che chung nyi shu bla brang rgyud khang du bzhag rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi sman sku che ba gcig dang /
thang ga byin can zhig rgyud khang steng du bzhugs /
mgon chos 'jigs gsum gyi zhal thang che ba mtha' shan spus legs sgrol dkar li ma khri tse gsum can /
rje rin po che'i li ma khri tse do /
rdo rje mi 'khrugs pa khri tse do /
rje rin po che dang sgrol ma'i sman sku byon legs rnams kwa ring dgon du bzhugs /
shing le khar gur mgon gsar bzhengs dang /
gong gi dus 'khor gyi thang sku che ba bzhag shel dgon du rgyal ba rdo rje 'chang la grub chen brgyad cus bskor ba'i thang ga che ba gong gsham zhal kheb bcas spus legs shig bzhag bis mdo dgon du thub sku gser zangs las grub pa tshon dgu ba zhig bzhag se chang dgon du jo'i sku khri rgyab yol can zhig bzhag hor tshang tsag tsag dgon par dngul rdo tshad lnga las grub pa'i kun rig dang /
'od dpag med /
mi 'khrugs pa thog tshad phyed dang gnyis pa can re bzhengs /
chos dpal zhing gi gzim khang du ston pa /
sgrol dkar /
'jam dbyangs dkar bo gsum rang gi lus tshad can re bzhengs /
des mtshon gzim khang der li ma dang sman sku bsdoms pas sku brnyan che chung brgya dang don bdun bzhugs /
yang mgon po'i sku li ma khri tse gsum can /
dngul rdo tshad drug gis blus pa'i sgrol ma nyer gcig dngul srang brgya dang don gsum gyis bsgrubs pa'i sgrol ljang gtso 'khor gsum /
sgrol ma khri tshad can rnams gzim khang der bzhugs /
dgung lo zhe dgu yan gyi sku brnyan li ma dang sman sku bcas drug cu lhag bla brang rgyud khang du bzhugs /
bla brang tshogs chen 'du khang gi rgya mthong gi logs ris thams cad tshwas zos te chud 'dza' ba thugs kyis ma bzod par sngon ma ji bzhin bzhengs nas legs mdzes su bsgrubs pa de la gyan thang dgu yod pas re re la dngul srang sum cu so drug re yon du phul /
chos dpal zhing du dus 'khor grwa tshang du dngul sgor drug cu re lngas dus kyi 'khor lo'i sku mi tshad tsam bzhengs te bzhag pa dang /
dngul sgor stong phrag gsum gyis sangs rgyas stong sku bzhengs shing log ris kyi thebs su'ang dngul srang drug cu phul /
bla brang brtsan khang du gyan thang gsum bzhag rgan rgya'i ban rgyar thang ga gsum bzhag nas ltung bshags btsugs /
gzhan yang gtong rtsa bzhag tho ni /
mtsho khar bzang spyod 'don rgyun la khron lnga bcu dang 'bru 'jags bzhi /
hor tshang tsag tsag dgon par bzang spyod gsar btsugs kyi thebs la khron drug brgya dang nas bre nyis brgya /
bkra shis sgar du bde mchog bdag 'jug gsar btsugs kyi rten khron brgya dang lnga bcu /
kha gya'i sgar rnying du ltung bshags phyag mchod gsar btsugs la khron brgya dang nyi shu /
gsang 'dus bdag 'jug gsar tshugs la nas bre bzhi brgya /
sgar gsar du byams khang gi thebs la khron stong /
mdzod dge dme po'i sgar gsar du khron stong /
chas pa rgya mkhar dgon zhig gsos 'theb la dngul sgor sum brgya dang gos ser bo kha bcu /
rje mi la'i sku tshon lnga can /
dngul gyi mchod rten dang sgrol dkar li ma khri tse gang re /
sa dmar dgon pa zhig gsos ched tho'i khron brgya dang bco lnga /
dngul ri'i ser sder ltung bshags gsar btsugs la mchod 'theb lnga bcu /
mar me'i rkong bu brgya /
dngul srang don lnga /
bla brang lo rnying lcags mkhar gyi 'theb la khron stong dang brgyad brgya bzhag gzhan yang sa bon du ma thebs pa du ma yod de dper na /
dmu dge bkra shis 'khor lo'i dgon du bka' 'gyur snar thang dpar ma tshar gcig gnang ba dang /
rje yab sras kyi gsung 'bum sogs gsung 'bum du ma bzhengs pa dang /
rje rin po che'i sku brnyan sogs sku brnyan dang mchod rten gyi gzungs gzhug la'ang bka' bstan sogs po ti stong phrag mang bo phul ba sogs shin tu mang /
khong gi zhal nas 'di dag kyang lag tu gang 'byor 'phral du phul ba ma gtogs /
gzhan la slong mo byas pa dang /
gzhan gyi rdzas rang gi yin khul byas pa med ces gsungs /
smras pa /
thos bsam sgom pa'i rin chen rdul mang las / /
nyer bskrun nyams rtogs rin chen lhun po la / /

ting 'dzin lha yi gzhal med khang chen dbus / /
zung 'jug zhabs zung rdo rje'i skyil krung bzhugs / /
bde stong ye shes rtse brgya 'bar ba yis / /
kun rtog lha min yongs kyi g.yul ngo bzlog /
thabs shes gser gyi chu 'dzin stug po las / /
dam chos sprin gyi me tog 'bum phab ste / /
log rtog zhugs chen gzhil dang lhan cig tu / /
sa lam rtogs pa'i rtsi bcud lo 'dab rgyas / /
khab len rdo chen lcags dang ma 'phrad par / /
lcags phye yongs su 'dren pa'i ngang tshul ltar / /
zhen pa gtan bral rigs brgya'i khyab bdag la / /
sgyu ma'i nor rdzas sprin bzhin 'du bar gyur / /
bya ba las kyi 'khor lo rtsibs stong gis / /
thub bstan gling chen bzhi la dbang bsgyur te / /
zung 'jug 'chi med gnas la dbang 'byor bas / /
nga las nu yi grags pa zil gyis mnan / /
zhes bla go rdo rje 'chang zhes yongs su grags pa rje btsun 'jigs med 'phrin las rgya mtsho dpal bzang bo'i rnam par thar ba dad pa'i padmo bzhad pa'i bden gtam nyi ma gzhon nu zhes bya ba las thog mtha' bar gsum gyi dge tshogs kun kyang bstan pa rgyas pa'i ched du bsngos te chos kyi 'khor lo bskor cing /
bya ba las kyi 'khor lo'i sgo nas kyang bstan 'gro'i don rlabs chen mdzad pa'i sarga ste bzhi ba'o / /
gnyis ba sku tshe 'di nyid kyi rnam thar rags rim thar chags su 'god pa /
'jigs bral rdo rje'i khri la dbang 'byor zhing / /

'phrin las lhun 'grub ga bur 'bum 'dzag pa / /

snyan pa'i tshig gi srad bur brgyu bar bya / /

mi nyag rab sgang dang drug go /
de dag la bod chol kha gsum du grags te /
mnga' ris gung thang nas sog la skya bo yan dbus gtsang chos kyi chol nas rgya'i mchod rten dkar bo yan mdo smad rta'i chol kha /
phyi ma mdo smad rta'i chol kha 'di la chu klung chen po rma chus bgos te mdo smad lho rgyud dang byang rgyud gnyis yod pa'i nang nas /
rje 'di ba 'khrungs yul ni mdo smad lho rgyud yin la /
de yang yum las bstan pa byang nas byang du dar bar 'gyur ro zhes lung bstan pa'i byang dar gnyis pa'i lte ba /
mdo sngags bstan pa'i 'byung gnas bla brang bkra shis 'khyil dang thag ha cang ring ba'i sa cha /
lung ba'i mdo rma klung phyogs la gtad cing /
phu shar lhor bltas pa'i lung ba mang du yod pa las /
yar nang tsho lngar grags pa'i ya gyal kwa ring zhes pa lung ba'i sked na ker langs kyi rdo ka ba lta bu zhig yod pa las btags pa yin zhing /
lo rgyus la lar brag ker langs 'di 'dra la dngos grub kyi rtags mtshan du bshad pa'ang yod ces dang /
la las bde mchog gi yul nyer bzhi'i nang gi bre ta bu ri yin zer /
chu shing 'dzoms la lo tog smin pa /
phu na 'brog gi rtswa sa'ang yod pas /
khang sa zhing sa sa yi dge / /
'thung chu zhing chu chu yi dge / /
gam 'brog rgyang 'brog 'brog gi dge / /
khang shing bud shing shing gi dge / /
khang rdo thab rdo rdo yi dge / /
zhes pa ltar gyi sa'i dge bcu tshang ba zhig go / /
yul mi rnams g.yo sgyu med pa /
ma bcos pa'i rang bzhin drang bo can /
rkun jag sogs spyod ngan gyi mig ltos mi byed cing /
dkon mchog la dad pa /
phal cher gzugs byad bzang zhing smra sgo yangs pa sogs chos sgrub pa'i rten 'os pa shas che ba'i yul sde de'i nang du rab byung bcu bzhi ba'i zad pa me pho stag gi lo'i tha skar gyi nya la dge mtshan gyi ltas dang bcas te rje 'di ba sku bltams /
rje 'di'i yab ni bis mdo'i dpon rgyud a brtan bu bdun gyi rgyud las a bo rta mgrin zer ba de yin gsungs /
a bo rta mgrin gyi pha mes brgyud rim ni dpal ldan 'bras spungs pa'i mi ser hor sog sde ma zhes pa sa dkar gdong drug gi dbus padma 'dab brgyad kyi lte bar a brtan zer ba srong btsan gdung rgyud du skyes pa zhig yod pas kho'i nu bo de ka'i dpon sar bzhag ste kho rang sa skyar phyin /
gong ma rin po ches bse'i ga'u kha sbyor dang /
gur mgon sku /
dar nag po kha gang dang bcas pa bstsal te bod sog gi sa mtshams su mngags /
de dus bla ma dka' bzhi ba bya bas dka' chen bcu drug phyir khrid pa gdan drangs /
bse'i ga'u da lta yod pa 'di yin gsungs pas khong gi dus su yod 'dug kyang da lta yod med cha ma 'tshal /
a brtan la rgyal mtshan dang bkra shis zer ba'i bu gnyis skyes /
bkra shis kyis dkyil 'khor sgar ba byas /
rgyal mtshan gyis gzhi bzung bas bu bdun skyes pa la a brtan bu bdun du grags /
khong gi yab a bo rta mgrin ni de'i rgyud pa zhig yin la /
mo ni ko'u a dpon zer pas byang rgyud kyi dgon sde rnams brlags zin nas mdo smad lho rgyud kyi dgon sde rnams gzhom du 'ongs pa khong gi yab de nyid kyis 'thab mos bzlog ste de phyogs bde 'jags su song ba yin zhing dpa' grags che /
lo rgyus zhib par 'bras spungs bis mdo'i mi tshan du yod zer /
des na khong gi gdung rus ni spyan ras gzigs dbang srong btsan sgam po'i gdung rgyud yin 'dug khong gi skyed yum lha mo byams ni khong gi sku phreng gong ma bla go bla sar 'jam dbyangs rgya mtsho'i tsha mo'i bu mo yin la yab yum rang bzhin drang zhing dkon mchog la dad pa dang ldan pa zhig yin /
khong gi ma yum gyis ko'u sde dpal ldan zhes pa chos dbyings stobs ldan rdo rje'i skye bar gleng ba de las 'ja' tshon snying bo'i pho ba 'jag tshugs ma la sbyangs pas rtags thon /
khong gi yab yum gnyis dga' 'dus su song yang khyo shug ma bsdeb pa'i bar der ma la khong mngal du zhugs /
ma yum rang gi spun zla mo lo ba zer ba'i khyim du bsdad pa'i tshe spun zla mo'i khyo ga snying byams rgyal zer ba des mdang nga'i rmi lam la nged kyi khyim gzhi der mchod rten chen po zhig yod pa'i mdun na lab tse zhig kyang byung ba rmis zer zhing /
de nub lha mo byams la khong 'khrungs pas snying byams rgyal dga' nas 'khur ba gsar ba gnyis btsos nas blta ru 'ongs pa red /
sku bltams dus mtshan mo yin yang khyim du mun pa med par dkar sangs kyis song stabs g.yog mo zhig yod pa des nam langs song bsam nas ldang bar brtsams pa na yul lugs kyis skar khung na bser bu 'gog ched zar ma'i rtswa'i phung bo brdzangs pa mthong pas mo skrag ste ldang ma nus zer /
khong gis khengs skyungs gnang nas bden rdzun ma shes gsungs kyang bden par nges te phyis kyi mdzad pa dang mthun par yod do / /
sngar mi tshang dbul phyug snyom pa zhig yin kyang phyis su za nyes 'thung nyes kyis nor rdzas zad /
gter zhig bsgrub pa la bum pa gas pa'i rten 'brel gyis tha mar dbul bor song pa red zer /
khong dgung lo bzhi lnga lta bu zhig la rgad po zhig yod pa shi nas pha ma tsho las kas brel te song shul du khong sgo khang lam srang du phag pa ma bu tsho dang lhan sdod byed dgos byung bas grib kyis thebs te zhal gyi tshems thams cad nag por gyur /
na nas sku 'da' la khad byung /
de'i tshe thar ba gling du khyer nas gser khang ba'i slob ma ri khrod pa zhig yod pas byabs khrus re gnang bas dwangs skyed cung thon yang khong gi mas nang phyags pa'i gad snyigs thab tu mer bsregs pas ma rang gi mig na nas zla ba phyed bcas gnyis tsam la thar ba gling du 'dug dgos byung /
de skabs khong stag ge tshang nas der bzhugs spong ba pa rnams la bde mchog dang 'jigs byed blo 'dzin gyi rgyugs bzhag pas gnas po dge slong gis 'dzin gshar byed pa khong gi snyan lam du son pas blo la thon nas dge slong des blo la ma thon pa dag khong gis gsal 'debs byed thub pa byung /
'di deng dus kyi rdzun lab kyis lung ston khul byed pa sogs la bag chags sad pa red zer ba dang mi 'dra bar sngon sbyangs kyi bag chags sad pa'i rtags mtshan yang dag go / /
'on kyang der bzhugs ring la sangs dwangs ma byung bas shel dgon du gdan drangs /
'di'i thad gsang rnam las / /
thar ba gling nas tho rengs dgon pa ru / /
byon pa'i lam bar nags tshal stug po'i dbus / /
mkha' 'gro ma rnams dgyes pa'i gar mdzad cing / /
rdo rje'i glu yis mchod pa mngon sum gzigs / /
zhes gsungs pa ltar gyi rnam thar ngo mtshar ba yod do / /
cung bzhugs stabs sku'i bsnyun dwangs mod khyim nas 'dzin mi chog pa'i lung bstan bab pas gzan sham 'dra ba re gsol te sngar gyi thar gling gi gnas po dge slong la bcol /
sngon gyi bag chags kyi dbang gis gzan sham gang mthong gyon pa dang /
khyad par sde de'i yul mi thams cad spyi khang du 'tshogs pa'i shul na skyed yum gyi ske rags ser bo zhig yod pa gzan gyi tshul du mnabs nas mi mang 'tshogs sar skyed ma'i gam du brgyugs pas kun bzhad gad thag ge bar song /
rgan po 'gas bzang bo'i bag chags can du 'dug zer /
de'i rkyen gyis bla ma zhig gi sprul sku red ces mi mang gi ngag la grags shing rgan po dag snang can dang bud med dad pa can 'ga' res mjal kha zhu ba yang yod 'dug thar ba gling nas khong dang na mnyam gyi byis pa 'ga' bcas srang bar nas rtse bzhin yod skabs shig khong stag ge tshang bla brang nas phebs pa red zer ba bltas pas khong lam ltag na yar gshegs /
rjes shig na zhabs zhu de rta la zhon bzhin 'ongs nas khong la khyod kyi ming la bla brang sku phyogs nas bskal bzang bstan pa zhes btags pa red ma brjed par gyis zhes zer bar khong gi thugs la bla brang sku phyogs nas nga mkhyen dogs yang mi 'dug na ming spos pa ci yin snyam pa zhig byung gsungs /
thar gling gi tshogs der dge slong min pa zhugs mi chog pas kwa ring dgon gyi tshogs la zhugs /
tshogs pas drug cu ba gsungs pas de la thugs zhen te zan brdzis pa ma zos par phyir khyer yong nas drug cu ba 'dra ba bcas te bsngo ba'i lad mo byas pa dran gsungs /
byis pa gzhan zhig dang mnyam du rtse mo byas te rdo leb gor mo zhig yod pa gzhan des rang 'thag bskor zer /
khong gis de ma red chos 'khor bskor zer nas ma 'cham par 'then 'khyer byed tshul khong stag ge tshang gi mdun du 'dug pas mthong nas stag ge tshang la zhus par dge ba'i bag chags yod pa kho yin 'dug gsungs /
de ltar skyes bu dam pa'i rang rtags du ma zhig mthong gshis bla go bla sar gyi skye sprul gyi tho yig nang bzhag go / /
de nas rab byung bco lnga ba'i chu sprel lor khong dgung grangs bdun du slebs skabs skyabs mgon thams cad mkhyen pa sku phren bzhi ba rje bskal bzang thub bstan dbang phyug dpal bzang bo'i thugs kun mkhyen ye shes kyis gzigs te gdan rabs lnga bcu ba bla go bla sar 'jam dbyangs rgya mtsho dpal bzang po'i sku'i skye bar thag bcad do / /
smras pa /
sgrib bral chos sku'i mkha' dbyings dag pa las / /
ye shes chos sku'i nyi zer 'bum shar te / /

dbyar gyi rnga gsang snyan po'i khengs pa bcom / /
de nas lo der khong rang yul na bzhugs yod tshe nyin zhig khong stag ge tshang phebs nas de kar khri brgyab nas khong khri thog tu gdan drangs te skyabs mgon rin po che'i phyag mdud dang kha dar phul te khri 'don gnang /
khong stag ge tshang gis de ka'i tsho mi rnams la khyed tshor gcig tu sgo mang bla ma chos dar tshang gi sku rtsar sprul sku 'di 'khrungs 'dug mi rgyud kyis ded na stag ge ngag dbang dge 'dun bstan 'dzin gyi sku nye'i rigs su 'dug gshis sprul sku 'di thag gcod kyi khur len thams cad rang gis bgyis te thag bcad pa 'di lags pas spyir kwa ring dgon grong /
sgos su gro'i thog 'bring gi tsho ba gnyis nas do dam khur len yang dag byas na sngon ma tshang gi rten dang sku chas gang yod da lan khyod tsho la sprod pa yin zhes gsung nan che ba gnang /
khong tshos dge rgan tshang la sku drin che dang thugs khur che bzhes gnang dgos zhes sogs zhus /
de nas stag ge tshang gi dpon pos rta dkar bo zhig gi chibs thog nas thar gling du gdan drangs /
de rjes 'gyang zhig nas thar gling de ka nas dgon grong kun la ston mo drangs te khri ston byas /
de skabs stag ge tshang gis khong la khyod kyis ltos dang mi mang bo 'tshogs e 'dug ces gsungs par khong phebs nas gzigs pas mi mang dga' tshom tshom byas 'dug pa gzigs nas khong stag ge tshang la 'dzin grwa 'dzin grwa byas nas 'tshogs 'dug zhus par khong la spyan cher gzigs nas phyogs 'di na 'dzin grwa zer ba'i ming tsam yang byis chung 'di 'dra'i thos yul du 'ong don med khyod la sus bshad pa yin gsungs /

rab mang gdul bya'i bsod nams zhing sa ru / /
rab mchog sprul ba'i bkod pa 'bum phrag rgyas / /
mtshan mor mun pa'i gos kyis g.yogs pa na / /
nyi ma gzhon nu'i 'od kyis bshus pa bzhin / /
dus kyi bshad sgrub 'od chen yal ba na / /
bshad sgrub 'od chen 'bar ba khyod nyid byon / /
bskal bzang thub pa yongs kyi bstan pa la / /
dbang 'byor lung rtogs mdzod kyis rab phyug pa / /
bstan pa'i bdag po skyabs mgon mchog de yi / /
zag med rnam kun mkhyen pas gsal ler gzigs / /
zab rgyas rtsibs stong gser gyi 'khor lo yis / /
thub bstan khyon la dbang bsgyur rgyal bo che / /
gong ma'i chos srid gser gyi khri 'phang la / /
mnga' gsol dge mtshan 'od kyis 'jig rten khyab / /
ces bla go rdo rje 'chang zhes yongs su grags pa rje btsun 'jigs med 'phrin las rgya mtsho dpal bzang bo'i rnam par thar ba dad pa'i padmo bzhad pa'i bden gtam nyi ma gzhon nu zhes bya ba las sku bltams shing /
mtshan gyi me tog rgyas te gong ma'i khri la mnga' gsol ba'i sarga ste lnga ba'o / /
chos grwar zhugs nas thos bsam gsha' ma byas te sgrub pa snying bo byed phyir gnas dben par gshegs pa'i sarga /
'jigs med lung rtogs bstan pa'i chu gter che / /
'phrin las rlabs kyis byis pa'i snying rtsa 'dar / /
gdams pa rin chen gter gyis yongs gang ba'i / /
bshes gnyen rgya mtsho che der slar yang 'dud / /
ded dpon mkhas pa'i gru rdzings legs bcos nas / /
rin chen gling nas rin chen dbang rgyal 'dren / /
dam pa'i bslab sdom rmang gzhi legs bting nas / /
thos bsam brtson pas zung 'jug nor bu len / /
rigs lam bye ba'i mdzod 'dzin mkhas mang dbus / /
me ltar 'bar ba'i shes rab rlabs chen gyis / /
thos bsam gnad la smin pa'i byung ba dag /
brjod pa mchod pa'i sprin gyis brjod par bya / /
dgung grangs dgu ba rab tshes shing pho khyi'i lor khong stag ge tshang gdan sa bkra shis 'khyil gyi rgyud khrid phebs dgos byung ba'i rjes su bla brang bkra shis 'khyil du hor zla bcu gcig pa'i tshes bcu bzhi la bslebs /
de nyin nyi ma byang bgrod kyi 'phel kha gsar rtsom dang 'grig pas rten 'brel ma bsgrig rang 'grig tu song 'dug /
dgung grangs bcu ba rab tshes shing mo phag gi lo'i gnam lo gsar bzhad la gong sa skyabs mgon mchog gi zhabs pad du gnam lo gsar tshes dgyes ston la thog ma'i mjal kha zhus /
thugs dgyes pa'i rnam pa cher mdzad de ka ra bag cha gcig sogs gnang /
phyis shig nas bla go bla sar chung chung zhig mjal ba khyod yin 'dug ces sku 'da' kha'i bar du yang yang gsungs pas thugs nas ma bor par yod gsungs /
lo de'i zla bzhi ba'i tshes bcu gsum la snyigs dus kyi 'phags pa nye bar 'khor chen po khong a khu rin po che shes rab rgya mtsho'i drung nas rab byung dang dge tshul bsgrubs pas khong gi gdul bya'i tha ma kun tu rgyu rab bzang lta bur song gsungs /
skyabs mgon rin po che lha sar phebs khar grwa tshang la tshe dbang gnang dus skyabs mgon rin po che mchog gi drung nas chos 'brel gyi thog ma thob /
dgung grangs bcu gcig pa rab tshes me pho byi ba'i lor glang pad ma'i bla ser zhes pa rdo rams pa 'phrin las rgya mtsho dge rgan du bsten nas bsdus gzhung sogs mtshan nyid la sbyangs pa dang chabs cig de lor sgo mang rin po che blo bzang tshul khrims rgya mtsho'i zhal snga las dam chos gyi bgo skal gyi thog ma srad rgyud bla ma'i rnal 'byor dga' ldan lha brgya ma'i gzab khrid zhib rgyas thob /
'jam dbyangs bla ma gung thang rin po che las kyang drag po sum dril gyi rjes gnang dang bzang spyod sogs kyi lung kha yar gsan /
dgung grangs bcu gnyis pa rab tshes me mo glang la dpyid tshes gnyis pa'i yar 'tshogs skabs chos grwar zhugs /
de skabs bsdus grwa blo 'dzin sel 'jug sgrub 'jug la slebs /
dbyar chos steng gong du zhus pa ltar 'gag ring thung gi dam bcar bzhengs pas rtsod pa 'gran zla dang bral ba byung bas gzur gnas dag gi yid dbang 'phrog pa byung /
dgun chos la bsdus grwa tshogs rgyugs su phul /
dgung grangs bcu gsum pa rab tshes sa pho stag la 'dzin grwa kha dog gong du grub mtha' rtsa ba dang 'grel ba don gsal thugs 'dzin gnang /
dgung grangs bcu bzhi ba rab tshes sa mo yos la 'dzin grwa bsdus 'bring /
de lor khyab bdag rdo rje sems dpa' chen po rje btsun ngag dbang thub bstan rgya mtsho dpal bzang bo las grub chen lo hu ba'i lugs kyi dpal 'khor lo sdom pa lha drug cu re gnyis pa'i dbang lta gon dang bcas gsan te gsang chen chos kyi sgor zhugs par mdzad /
de nas bzung bka' chos nam yod chad med lta bur phebs te gsan bzhes mdzad pa'i sdom grangs gong du bkod pa ltar la zhal nas bka' drin snying la lci zhes gsungs /
de'i dgun ngor 'grel ba don gsal dang grub mtha' rtsa ba tshogs rgyugs su phul /
dgung grangs bco lnga ba rab tshes lcags pho 'brug la bsdus chen du slebs /
dpyid yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i mnga' bdag drin can bla ma zhang ston bstan pa rgya mtsho dpal bzang bo'i zhabs rdul spyi bor bsten pa'i skal bzang thob ste bstan pa'i 'jug sgo skyabs 'gro'i khrid dang /
dga' ldan lha brgya ma dang /
gang blo ma sogs lung phran kha yar thob gsungs /
de skabs lo'i 'brug skad thog mar byung bas rten 'brel legs zhes phebs /
de nas yang bka' chos nam yod la chud pa'i bka' drin bskyangs shing /
gzigs dpe gang dgos 'tshol ba dang /
gsung rtsom nyung shas 'bri ba'i phyag g.yog zhu ba sogs kyi skal ba'ang thob ces gsungs /
lo de'i dgun ngor blo rtags don bdun cu dang bcas pa'i tshogs rgyugs phul /
dgung grangs bcu drug pa rab tshes lcags mo sbrul la rtags rigs 'dzin grwar slebs ste blo rig tshogs gling gnang ba dang gzhung rgyugs phul /
dgung grangs bcu bdun pa rab tshes chu pho rta'i lor gzhung gsar du slebs nas dge 'dun nyi shu gsar rtsod dang dus 'grig pas zla gnyis pa'i nyer drug gi bar chos grwar phebs /
de skabs dge rgan tshang nas da khyod a lags rin po che nas bka' 'gyur gyi lung gnang ba nyan du song /
the'u blo bzang gi gam nas sdod la dpe ltas kyang le shor med pa gyis zhes gsungs pa ltar bka' 'gyur gyi lung nyan te mdo dran pa nyer bzhag gi bar song zin pas ra dum pa nas bzung rdzogs par nyan /
sngon stag ge tshang nas khyod tshogs chos 'grim pa la khang mig chung ngu zhig gis yong gsungs pa ltar /
'di lor khang ba snga ma btsong ste khang chung zhig tu spos /
de phyin kha smras gleng brjod mang ba sogs dang yang dgos khams ma snyoms par brten gro ra tshang mo ma rno shos su grags pas brtag pa zhus par /
rta mgrin gyi bsnyen pa dang gur drag dang rta mgrin 'khor lo sham bu can yod pas de skor zer /
de 'phral khong rang nyid rta mgrin gyi bsnyen par bzhugs pa'i mnal lam du khong dang khong gi 'dzin grwa bcas bsdus chen gyi go sar rtsod pa byed pa la khong a lags rin po che glo bur du phebs byung ba zhal dmar zhing zil che ba khro tshul gyis spyan hrig hrig phyogs kun gzigs pas khong gi 'dzin grwa'i smad sog ma cig zer ba de la brdung rdeg mang bo gnang ba zhig rmis /
bsnyen pa grol tshe khams kyang rang sar cung babs /
'khor lo de 'bad pas bskor bas thams cad nas phyi phyir mi 'tsham par gyur bas 'khor los lan par shes nas gzhan la byin /
lha khyad par ba yin nges la nged rang la snga 'gyur phyogs 'di la las 'phro ngan pas 'brel med pa go gsungs /
rdo rje 'chang mkhan rin po che ngag dbang dge legs tshang ngag dbang thub bstan rgya mtsho de nyid kyis dus 'khor dbang skur skabs sde khri sprul ba'i sku 'jigs med bstan pa'i nyi ma tshang nas khong la nged rang gnyis sham+b+ha lar mnyam 'gro byed pas de'i rten 'brel du dbang gi skabs thams cad du lhan sdod lhan 'gro zhes gsungs nas khong a lags rin po ches dge tshal sgrub skabs gnang ba'i 'jam dpal mtshan brjod gser bris shig yod pa gnang ste chos kyi rgyal mtshan legs par 'dzugs zhes pa'i bar thon zhes phebs pa bzhin byas /
rjes shig la yi ge zhig gnang bar khyod bla rgan sma ra dkar po can zhig tu ma gyur bar du 'gro ba'i skabs med ces phebs /
skyes bu dam pa zhig yin nges la byis pa mno bsam med pa'i tshul bzhes pa'i skabs red snyam yang phyis sog yul du byon skabs lan gru nas kha dar zhig bskur te da bud song bde bar gyis zhes phebs 'dug pa sogs sog yul du byon pa'i don las ma go mod khong zhing gzhan du dgongs pa gtad pa dang /
nga rang gi tshe tshad bcas gsungs pa la nges pa rnyed ces gsungs /
'di yang dam pa gnyis ka'i rtogs pa'i mngon rtags yin te sde khri rin po ches ma 'ongs lung bstan gnang ba ji bzhin thog tu bab pa dang /
rje 'di bas kyang sde khri rin po che skyes bu dam pa yin par mkhyen cing lung bstan don thugs su chud pas so / /
dgung grangs bco brgyad pa rab tshes chu mo lug gi lor 'dzin grwa gzhung gong du slebs /
'dzin skyor dpe khrid sogs dang /
sgo mang rin po che las bde lam gyi khrid nyin bdun /
'jigs byed dpa' cig bde mchog lo hu ba dang dril bu lha lnga /
'dus pa lugs gnyis dang 'jig rten dbang phyug 'khor chen /
mngon byang /
zab don snyan brgyud kyi gcod dbang sogs dbang du ma dang /
rnam sras bka' bco lnga sogs rjes gnang mang po gsan /
skyabs mgon rin po che sku 'bum mkhan por bzhugs pa'i mtshams zhus lta bur khong stag ge tshang phebs te gong sa mchog gi ma yum dang /
dpon po tshang sogs la 'phros gleng mang bo byed skabs khong rin po che 'di ba tsha kan be shing gi khrir phebs dgos kyi gros mgo bton /
de'i don rnams sba gsang med par stag ge tshang gis khong la gsungs pas khong rin po che 'di bas thugs la shar tshul gsungs pa ni /
rgyal dbang bdun pas / /
chos med chos par rlom pa'i bzang rdzu mkhan bdag gi / /
las ngan 'khrul ngor shar ba'i snang tshul la bltas na / /
thams cad sdug bsngal bskyed pa'i snon pa ru 'dug pa / /
zhes gsungs pa bzhin kha dog dkar dmar gong bsdus 'bring gsum ma gtogs lo brgyad kyi steng nas da bar lo re bzhin ston zla gnyis sam phyed dang gnyis lta bu re la nas bsod ces sbrang 'khyams la ma song dus mi gda' /
min kyang nged rang khri zur sprul sku yin rgyu ba byas /
khong yang khri thon zin du song gshis nang gcig nas khral mgo gnyis bsdu ba sogs kyi dka' las la thug pas dpe shog ldebs gsum tsam yang 'dzin skyor yid phebs pa zhig mi 'byung bas phyi nas kyang gzhung lugs la sbyang ba'i skal ba lta ci kha ton mag mug re byed rgyu'i bsod nams yang mi 'dug bde gsang sogs lhag lha 'di rnams la mtshams bsnyen sgrub lta bu re byed rgyu ma byung na de bas phongs tshab che ba mi 'dug snyam yid mi bde zhes gsungs pa yang gong du bshad pa ltar gyi rnam thar bla na med pa'o / /
lo de'i dgun nas bzung ste phar phyin skabs dang bo tshogs rgyugs la phul /
dgung grangs bcu dgu ba rab tshes shing pho sprel lor 'dzin grwa skabs dang bor slebs /
dpe khrid dpe bltas 'dzin skyor sogs sngar rgyun bzhin gnang thog a khu rin po che zhang ston bstan pa rgya mtsho'i zhal snga las khong sgo mang rin po che dang lhan du rgyal thang ba bsam gtan 'od zer gyi gcod skor gyi lung /
tA ra na tha'i dbang chog steng nas dbang dang lung sogs du ma dang /
dus 'khor bskyed rim gyi bshad lung gnang ba rnams gsan /
sgo mang rin po che las stag phu'i sgrol ma phyi nang gnyis kyi dbang gnyis thig le bcu drug 'jigs gsang mkha' spyod sogs kyi sngags btu /
paN chen bstan pa'i nyi ma'i gsung 'bum gyi lung sogs chos bka' rgya cher gsan /
rig byed ma'i don kun 'grub pa'i 'khor lo gsar sgrub dang yi ge'i sngags kyi lag 'khor zhib par bskrun te khong sgo mang rin po cher phul bas dgyes nyams dang bcas thugs mkho che byon nas bdag gir bzhes /
'dzin grwa gtugs la bzhengs te rtags gsal ya mtshan pa btang pas rigs lung cher song /
drang nges tshogs gleng babs te dbyar chos chen mor dam bca' sogs gshis phyin par gnang /
dbyar chos grol 'phral phar phyin ston mo'i ched du 'brog phyogs su shol bcas zla ba gnyis lhag 'bul sdud du phebs stabs tshogs gleng dngos gzhi gnang rgyu ma song /
dgun ngor bde gsang gnyis sogs lhag lha du ma zhig gi bsnyen pa btang /
dgung grangs nyi shu ba rab tshes shing mo byi lo la 'dzin grwa skabs bzhi bar slebs /
dpyid dus su stong skor rab 'byams pa sbyin pa rgya mtshos nan tan chen po byas te zhus ngor bde mchog gi dbang gnang /
'di dbang gnang ba'i thog ma yin 'dra /
drug pa'i tshes drug la khong sgo mang rin po che nas mkhan slob sbrags ma dang khong nyid kyi mchod dpon dge slong dkon mchog rgya mtsho bas gsang ston /
khong zhal snga nas lung rtogs rgya mtsho sogs kyis kha skong mdzad nas bsnyen par rdzogs te thugs rgyud sdom pa gsum gyis yongs su gtams pas gsum ldan rdo rje 'dzin pa chen por gyur /
zla bcu ba'i nyer lnga la 'dzin grwar phar phyin ston mo'i bsnyen bkur bla na med pa gnang /
phar phyin dam bca'i skabs rtags gsal btang tshul sogs gong du thos pa rgya chen btsal ba'i rnam thar brjod pa'i skabs su brjod zin pa ltar rtsod pa phyogs chen gnang bar dam bca' khas len yang dag par gnang /
dam bca' tshar nas sngar bsnyen pa ma song ba'i lhag lha 'ga' dang /
nang mtshams zhag bdun ma sogs gnang /
dgung grangs nyer gcig pa rab tshes me pho khyi'i lo la smon lam steng brag dkar phyogs su gnyan khrod la phebs /
gnas khang du thog ma'i bdun mtshams gnang ba dang /
bkra shis 'khyil zer ba'i mis 'grim 'grul med pa'i 'gol yangs shig yod pa der bar gyi bdun mtshams gnang /
mtsho kha nas tha ma'i bdun mtshams gnang ste chu stod zla ba'i mar ngo'i tshes bcur sbyin sreg gnang nas grub 'phral gdan sar phyir phebs /
khong gis khengs skyungs gnang ste rnam rtog gi 'gyur ba ches cher brtas pa la gnyen pos 'bur 'joms kyis ma chum pas yi mug ldang ba zhig las ma byung gsungs kyang gsang rnam las /
mkha' 'gro'i thugs bcud phung bo zan bsgyur chos / /
thabs shes zab mo gcod gyis nyams bzhes gyis / /
phra rags bdud tshogs dbyings su bskrad dang lhan / /
gzung 'dzin rnam rtog cho 'phrul rang sar dag /
ces gsungs pa ltar lags la /
gdan sar slebs 'phral zhal snga nas a khu zhang rin po cher mjal bar /
a khu rin po che'i zhal nas dpyid 'dir khyod ma bsdad pa de ches phangs khong a lags rin po che nas chos rgyun shin tu dkon pa 'ga' zhig gnang song gsungs /
de rjes cher ma 'gyang par zhwa dmar rin po che phebs te khong a khu tshang la rje'i bstod 'grel dang sbyong rgyud dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis sogs dang /
khong a lags rin po che la shar ba'i lam rim /
snying bo don gsum /
rngog dkyil bdun sogs zhus pa khong gis kyang gsan /
de skabs tshe 'di'i rten bzhengs kyi thog ma a lags rin po che dang /
sgo mang rin po che /
bde mchog mkha' spyod ma /
zhal bzhi ba rnams kyi tsa ka li re bzhengs te khong sgo mang rin po cher lhag gnas zhus par nyin shas zhog gsungs pas sku drung du bzhag khong nyid kyis zhal thang sgros la snum thigs shig lhung song ba sku nye nas gzhan gyi ca ka brdzad zhus par grwa rkyang gi kha la snum thigs re 'gos na bzang mod gsungs /
de phyin zas nor gyis mi phongs pa zhig 'ongs pa de ka'i byin rlabs dang rten 'brel du 'khums zhes gsungs /
sngar nas bla ma nang chen gyi 'dzin bdag la thugs log ste /
zhe sa ngo 'dzin dgos pa'i dpon po yang med la / /
zhes sogs sho lo ka gcig gi don ltar ri khrod pa tsho'i sgom sgrub la bar chad med cing thos don sgrub pa la gzhol bas thugs drangs te rang yang de 'dra ba zhig byung na snyam pa las thugs la gzhan 'char rgyu med /
yin kyang gsar bu lo chung gi blo la phug gtad med pas dpal mgon zhal bzhi ba rang la 'go zhing ltas mtshan gsal ngom zhig yod pas dus 'khor grwa tshang du bsang zhig btang ste snyan shal zhig phul ba logs bris kyi mgon po zhal gyi mche ba bzhi'i rtse mor nyin shas bzung bas rang la'ang spobs pa skyes te khong zhang rin po cher 'dun gros zhus par lan du khyod kyang mi ring bar phyogs yas mas gang rigs shig tu 'gro dgos pa nges can pas de bas gzhan dben pa re bsten nas dge sbyor bya nus na kho bo shin tu dga' /
sngar nged kyi sems ngor khyod nga'i rtsar zhig tu bzung ste rgyud par lo shas 'gror bcug na snyam pa yod mod /
don smin zhig mi yong ba ngo shes zhes phebs /
zhes gsungs pa 'di dag ni rgyal bu don kun grub pas grong khyer gyi sgo bzhi nas skye rga na 'chi dang /
dge slong gzigs pa'i rkyen gyis rgyal srid dor ba'i rnam par thar ba dang shin tu mtshungs so / /
de nas zhwa dmar rin po cher zhu sna bcol te reb kong sku zhabs a rol rin po cher de ka'i ri khrod du zhugs rgyu zhus par yong gsungs zhes phebs te tshe sgrub /
tA re /
myur mdzad ma sogs rim gro kha yar bsgrubs /
a rol tshang nas bis mdor sems bskyed mchod pa gnang rgyu yin pas de skabs 'byor ba gyis zhes phebs sgo bstsal /
rgyu mtshan khong a khu zhang ston rin po che tshang la zhus par zhal nas rang re'i sku zhabs tshang la'ang gtan ma zhus par song na khong gi thugs kyi dgongs par ci 'char mi shes pas lan gcig zhus par drag gsungs pa ltar khong mgo log phyogs su bzhugs pa la 'phrin zhus par mi 'gyang bar dgon thog tu sleb nges yin pas de'i bar sdod dang gros byed ces phebs par nyan te bcu ba'i tshes kyi bar 'gro rgyu ma byung gsungs /
phyi nas zhus par reb kong yin dgos mi 'dug 'di ka'i ri khrod bkra shis dge 'phel du bzhugs dang khad nye spro bde sogs su yod ces dgongs pa ma grol /

de dus a rol rin po ches byin gyis reb kong phyogs kyi ri khrod pa tsho sgrub tshugs legs pa chos kyi mthun rkyen ran pa sogs kyis re ba che yang don smin ma byung bas zhe chad dang yi mug ldang yang tshangs pa'i lung bstan las /

zhal nas ri khrod du rkang tshugs pa dang phyag rdor 'khor chen nam rta mgrin gang rigs kyi bsnyen pa zhig thongs gsungs pa ltar mgo zla ba'i tshes la dge 'phel ri khrod der ma 'gyang bar 'khor chen gyi bsnyen pa sbyin sreg bcas grub par gnang /
khong ri khrod du phebs khar a khu rin po cher sbyor ba'i chos drug nyams su bstar tshul lag len zhib gsal zhus pas gnang ste zhal nas lam sne re re nas 'bad pas sbyang na skye skye 'dra'ang de bas thun re re la mdo sngags yongs su rdzogs pa'i gnad tshang ba re gshar sbyang byas na dga' mod ces gsungs pa thugs la bcangs te ri khrod nas mdo sngags yongs su rdzogs pa la dpyad sgom byas te rtogs pa cher 'phel mod 'on kyang khong gis khengs skyungs gnang ste gsung ba /
rang la pho skyes na reb khong yin dgos pa'i nges pa med snyam nas nyams len zhig la 'bungs blo byas kyang rgyal dbang bdun pas /
bstan bcos man ngag rnams kyis dag byas kyang / /
nges par blo ngan rab dwangs nyid mi 'gyur / /
ga bur tshogs kyis yongs su bsgos gyur kyang / /
mi bzad sgog pa rang gi dri mi gtong / /
zhes gsungs pa ltar /
thog med nas ngan goms kyis sems nang du mi khug pas re dogs dang dga' sdug chu gnyer bzhin dkrigs shing khyad par sems kyi bde sdug kun nang rnam rtog gi cho 'phrul du song bas sems la 'khu 'khrigs byung na bdag 'dzin yul nas thon /
nang 'dre rang sems thul na phyi 'dre stong bar yal /
zhes pa ltar dgos nges shar mod sems rgyud r+wa ltar gyong ba la sen mo zhig ma thebs zhes gsungs pa khengs skyungs tshul gyis gdul bya rnams la man ngag gi mthil bstan pa yin no / /
dgung grangs nyer gnyis pa rab tshes me mo phag gi lor rang 'gar bsdad pas dgos pa mi 'dug dgongs nas rgyun bsnyen lta bur bde mchog lo hu ba'i cho ga dang 'brel bar ka ra ka ra 'bum phrag gcig de'i bdag 'jug brgya rtsa brgyad rnams grub 'phral sbyin sreg stong phrag gcig phul /
de nas lo phyed lhag tsam la de ka'i ri khrod bkra shis dge 'phel gyi gnas brtan 'grig bdag gis khur bzhes te 'grig lam nyams pa thams cad sor chud dang /
ma nyams pa gong 'phel btang /
dbyar sgom khang bde chen 'od gsal du 'dus pa spyi dang lhan nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i rim gnyis kyi khrid kyang nyan /
nyin zhig skyabs mgon mchog gi sku mdun du phebs par /
de ring khyod 'dir 'ongs pa la bltas sam mdang nga'i rmi lam du zhes sogs mkhas mchog yon tan 'od kyi skye bar lung bstan pa sogs gong du brjod zin to / /
dgung grangs nyer gsum pa rab tshes sa pho byi ba'i lo la skyabs mgon mchog ri khrod du byon pa'i zhar la khong gi shar tu phebs /
dpe rnams bam gzigs gyis nang nas dpa' bo gtsug lag 'phreng ba'i chab shog pod gcig dang dril bu lus dkyil gyi bla ma'i rnal 'byor sogs bzhes te phebs /
de'i skabs skyabs mgon mchog nas khong la me tog bcud len zhig la sdod rgyu yin na legs gsungs /
khong gis lto gdung gis dka' tshul zhus par ma zer ma mtha' smon lam kyi rten du khrid cig yin yang nyon zhes gsungs stabs /
khong a lags rin po cher dge 'dun rgya mtsho'i rim lnga dben sa ba'i chu bcud len steng nas khrid cig kyang nyan /
khong a khu rin po che zhang tshang la bsnyen sgrub sbrags ma'i khrid zhus te khrums stod zla ba'i tshes nyer dgu nas 'jigs byed bsnyen chen la bsdad /
'jam dbyangs zhi ba'i bsnyen pa 'bum lta bu sngon du btang na bar chad chung zhes khong a khu rdo rje 'chang gis gsungs pa bzhin byas /
'di skabs nang gcig thun dang po grol 'phral ra bar kha ba phyags phyir phebs pa na gzigs snang khyad par can byung ba gong du brjod pa ltar la /

mgon chos /
lha mo rnam sras sogs thugs 'dzin gnang /
de rjes skyabs mgon mchog khong gi spyil bur byon nas ka ma la dang zla ba'i dkyil 'khor steng zhes pa'i dbu can gyi sgrol dkar bstod pa zhig ljags rtsom mdzad nas zhu ba po khyod yin rgyu byas gsungs te ri khrod kyi tshogs su btsugs /
ma 'gyang bar sgrol dkar gyi bsnyen pa zhig gyis zhes gsungs pa dang du blangs te sgom khang gong nas sgrol dkar gyi bsnyen pa gnang /
bsnyen pa grub 'phral ri khrod du slebs pa na shul du nged kyi steng nas zing cha che tsam zhig bslangs 'dug kyang de ma thag mtshams bsdams nas chos rgyal gyi bsnyen pa zhig btang ste grol dus gong sa mchog gi byin gyis zing cha rang yal du song 'dug ces gsungs pa'i don gong du zhus pa ltar la /
sgrol dkar bsnyen pa de yang bstan 'gro'i don du sku tshe brtan pa'i ched du skyabs mgon mchog gis snyan bskul gnang par nges te khong gi zhal nas /
tshe'i bar chad cig yod pa bla ma dang 'phags ma'i byin rlabs kyis nyer 'tshe phra mo de tsam gyis bzlog pa yin mchi snyam du dad pa kha zhe med pa zhig skyes zhes gsungs /
lo de'i ston dgun yang bskyar nA ro mkha' spyod dang /

he ru ka'i yig brgya 'bum grangs bsags /

rgyal zla ba'i bcu gnyis la mtshams khongs su chud pa byas te thar ba rtse mi med pa'i 'gol gnas su bsdad gshis de ka nas bsnyen sgrub sprags ma bcu cha sbyin sreg rnams grub par byas /
de'i gzhi bsnyen skabs nub cig srod thun la rkyen med par gting nas ngu snying zhig 'ongs nas mang bo ngus /

srid dang zhi ba ro mnyam nyid gyur ba'i / /

sngar nas khang chung skyid nge ba zhig yin mod da cha lhag par mtshams bsnyen sgrub mang bo byas pa'i rkyen gyis byin chags shing bag dro ba zhig tu gyur 'dug rtsig ngos 'di la dur khrod mtshan nyid tshang ba zhig dang dkar dmar nag pa'i thig le gsum phris zhes gsungs 'dug yang rjes shig skyabs mgon mchog byon nas gsol ja bzhes zin 'phral gnyid bro gsungs nas gzims la cung zad yur te thugs sangs pa dang mdun 'dir rgya gling zhig 'dug ste da lta gtong gin mi 'dug ces gsungs /

cod pan cha /

der bzhugs dge 'dun rnams kyis bde mchog rkyang ba las bdag 'jug mi mdzad pa la dong tse khron brgya thebs su gnang ste phyi nas tshes bcu nam yod la bdag 'jug gsung rgyun btsugs /
de ka'i sa'i tshe kyi dre'u skyel mi bcas gan go'i dgon par phyag phebs /
der zhag gcig gnas 'brel byas te se tha zir 'byor /

dgung grangs nyer bdun pa rab tshes chu pho 'brug la gong sa rin po che sgom khang du bzhugs pa la ngam rdzong snyan brgyud kyi dbang zhus pas co ne a mo de skabs sku mdun na bcar bzhugs kyis yod pas de'ang tshud dgos byung ste nged rang gnyis char la tshes bcu'i nyin gsungs /
'di skyabs mgon mchog gi gsang rnam las /
nyin gcig rmi lam du zhes sogs gsungs pa'i don gong du brjod zin pa ltar ro / /

kha skong sbyin sreg skabs glo bur du 'brug grags thog tshag ser ba drag po byung ba sogs 'tshubs ltas che ba byung 'dug de nas lo gcig tsam la rgyun pa'i nyams len gnang /

snyan brgyud dgos na dril bu lus dkyil 'di 'jam mgon chos kyi rgyal bo dang dben sa grub thob mched sogs kyi nyams bzhes yin pas dben sa snyan brgyud rang yin zhes bkyon pas de nas brtsams tshes bcu re lta bu la bton kyang gong sa mchog nas 'da' kha'i bar rgyang bskyur ma byed ces yang yang gsungs pas do gal che ba zhig yin nges lags zhes gsungs 'dug ston mjug gong sa mchog sgom khang du phebs /
yang shag tu phebs te gsol ja gung tshigs sogs thams cad bzhes te rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i rtsa dbu ma che ba'i nyams khrid sogs mkha' spyod skor gyi man ngag kha yar lung bcas bstsal /
khong gis gong sa mchog 'di ba'i chos kyi bka' drin dang tha na sos bde gu yangs su tshe gang bor 'dug rgyu byung ba tshun gang gi bka' drin yin pas drin lan gzhal dka' bar yod ces gsungs /
de yang yin te gzhon dus nas skal ldan gyi slob mar gzigs te man ngag snyan brgyud rnams phangs med du bstsal nas nang thugs kyi sras gcig pur gyur /

nyin de'i dgong mor sgom khang du phyir gshegs te phyag yig cig gnang ba'i ngos na kye rdo rje 'di lho brag mar ba dang sa skya'i rje btsun gong ma rim byon rnams kyi thugs dam gyi gtso bo yin pas 'di la bsnyen pa zhig thongs /
rdo rje gdan bzhi 'di yang mar ston chos kyi blo gros dang rngog chos sku rdo rje sogs kyi thugs dam zhe gtsigs che ba yin pas 'di la'ang bsnyen pa zhig thongs zhes phebs 'dug da lta bsam na de ka nged kyi nang du khong phebs pa'i tha mar song 'dug pas yid skyo ba tshad las 'das zhes gsungs /

dur khrod bdag po /

bu'i spyi don snye ma dang /

zhes gsungs pa ltar khong rin po che 'di bas 'jig rten pa'i mi drag sku drag sogs la zhe sa ngo 'dzin mig sngar mdzes chos sogs gang yang mi byed stabs gong sa mchog gi zhabs zhu gsar spos pa dag dang mi chen 'ga' zhig gi sgra dang sdeb sbyor sogs bslab pa la bsnyad btags te rje 'di ba ri khrod du mi bzhugs zer zhing gong sa mchog la'ang snyan phra zhus pa sogs kyis 'bo ra'i sngon po thang gi khrir bsko bzhag byas /

zhes lung bstan pa'i dus la bab pa dang ri khrod nas mtshams bsnyen sgrub sogs nyams len mtha' chod pa gnang bas nyams rtogs gong du 'phel te gzhan don byed pa'i dus la bab pa na slar dpal ldan bkra shis 'khyil du phyag phebs te bla ma rnam pa'i bka' chos gang gsung gsan /
khong gi zhal nas dgon mtha' 'dir bka' chos gang gnang chag med du nyan rgyu byung ba lha dang bla ma'i byin rlabs dang thugs rjer shes zhes gsungs pa dang /

khong dgung grangs nyer dgu'i skabs 'dir khong dbal mang rin po che srid skyong la bzhugs pa dang bsdongs nas sngar gyi 'phros nas gang min gyi ngan spyod mang po dgos med du bsham na yang khong skyabs rje dbal mang rin po che nyid g.yo 'gul ma byung ba'i rkyen gyis kho rang tsho'i ngan spyod de mtha' rdugs su gyur /
de skabs sdang sems khong du zhugs pas bla dpon 'gas dpung sgril gyi zhu phras gong sa mchog nyid kyang mdzad dka'i mtshams su bskyal /
de skabs khong rin po che 'di ba gnas chung la bsang gtong du phebs par lam nas shog bu gru bzhi zhig rnyed nas gzigs pas logs shig na rgya gser gyis bris pa'i stag nyams dod pa zhig dang rgyab tu dbu 'bab rgya mtsho zhes pa'i yi ge zhig yod pas da ni chos skyong gi 'phrin las kyis mi skyon pa ngo shes snyam pa byung ba bzhin khyi rgan ku co che ba rang phung ber ka'i char 'bod du song /
zhes gsungs /
dgung grangs sum cu ba rab tshes shing mo lug gi lor mgo log dkon bkra'i chos mdzad zer ba bla brang phyag mdzod du bzhag pas chab srid kyi byed pa bo kho gcig pur gyur pas bde 'jags byung /
'di ni mgo log dkon bkra tshang yin la khong grwa sar phebs nas 'bras spungs sgo mang grwa tshang du zhugs te chos mdzad btang bas dkon bkra'i chos mdzad ces grags /
khong gong sa skyabs mgon mchog gi tsha bu yin te rang rnam las tsha bu mdzod pa zhes gsungs /
skyabs mgon mchog chab srid thog mdzad dka' byung skabs dkon bkra'i chos mdzad la yi ge btang ste nga la grogs byed du khyod yong dgos zhes bka' nan che bas kho yong nas lo bcur bla brang phyag mdzod byas zer /
de'i bar skyabs mgon mchog stod gangs ri sogs su gnas gzigs la phebs /
phyag mdzod thugs zin byung zer /
lo 'di'i dpyid ka khong rin po che 'di ba sho ba'i rta mgrin dang len spa san du phyag skor dang gnas gzigs la phebs /
zhal snga nas sgo mang rin po che las rje'i gsung 'bum gyi lung ta pod yan chad song ba'i mtshams nas gdan 'dren pa byung bar brten dbyar ston khong gi 'khrungs yul kwa ring du phebs /
de kar bzhugs skabs su sgo mang rin po ches khong la 'jam dkar gyi bsnyen pa zhig gyis zhes gsung phebs /
de don a khu rin po che la zhus pas a khu rin po che nas khyod shes rab chung bas a lags tshang nas 'jam dkar thon gsungs pa ma red /
khyod rgyud ha cang rtsub cing gyong bas je 'jam la e 'gro dgongs pa red ces gsungs /
de nas bzung bya rgyud rang skad ltar bsnyen pa skabs skabs su btang ba tshar bcu song /
khong a khu rin po ches khyod shes rab chung bas a lags tshang nas 'jam dkar thon gsungs pa ma red ces pa ni snang tshod la'ang shes rab ha cang che bar gsungs pa dang khyod rgyud ha cang rtsub cing gyong bas je 'jam la e 'gro dgongs pa red ces pa ni po to ba chen pos /
gyong du bya zhing 'gro dka' bya / /
zhes gsungs pa ltar bka' gdams gong ma'i rnam thar bdag gir bzhes pa bstan pa yin no / /
gzhan yang khong a khu rin po che'i thugs kyi sras gcig pur gyur pas rjes su bzung tshul gong du bshes gnyen bsten tshul gyi skabs su cung zad bshad mod gal po che la nan tan gyi tshul du 'dir dgung lo sum cu'i dkyus su yod pa thar chags su 'god par bya ste /
yang nyin gcig a khu rin po cher mjal du phebs skabs zhal nas mi dang ma 'grog par 'dug mi thub /
su dang 'grogs kyang skyon ye med pa zhig gtan mi srid mi dang 'grig rgyu gal che cung zad re la bsnyad btags nas spo lang gi ma bsdad na bzang /
res gcig gnyis re la bsran btsugs te bsdad na spangs pa min yang mi mngon pa zhig tu 'gro rgyu yod /
kha ton mag mug zhig 'don rgyu las dpe char blta ba gtso bo gyis /
dpe ltas la tshogs bsags sgrib sbyong thams cad kyi gnad yod 'dug pas gal chen gyis /

zhes bla go rdo rje 'chang zhes yongs su grags pa rje btsun 'jigs med 'phrin las rgya mtsho dpal bzang bo'i rnam par thar ba dad pa'i padmo bzhad pa'i bden gtam nyi ma gzhon nu zhes bya ba las skyabs mgon sku phreng bzhi ba zhal bzhugs pa'i ring la bka' gsung dang du blangs te mdo sngags dam chos kyi char chen phab nas sangs rgyas bstan pa'i srog bzung ba'i sarga ste brgyad pa'o / /

skyabs mgon thams cad mkhyen pa rje bskal bzang thub bstan dbang phyug dpal bzang bo dgongs pa rdzogs rjes srid skyong dbal mang rin po che 'jam dbyangs bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho dang mkhan chen ngag dbang dge legs pa'i yang sprul bskal bzang mkhas grub rgya mtsho /
bsod grags sprul ba'i sku rin po che 'jigs med bsod nams rgya mtsho ste dam pa gsum gyis bskul ba bzhin skyabs mgon mchog gi rnam thar kha skong shes ldan yid kyi dga' ston rin chen 'phreng ba'i mdzes rgyan zhes bya ba'i legs bshad rmad du byung ba ljags rtsom mdzad pa dang sku gdung rin po che zhugs 'bul sogs la yang khur len yang dag mdzad /
de nas yang bla ma rnam pas bstan pa'i bdag por mnga' gsol ba bzhin mu mthud de bar ma chad par chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i tshul ni /
lo de'i zla ba gsum pa'i tshes bcu gsum nas nyin lngar sgrub thabs rin 'byung gi lung dang gung thang 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyis mdzad pa'i gtor bsngos nas dag chos dbyings ma'i lung gnang /
