sa lugs 'jam dbyangs dmar ser /
sgrol dkar 'od zer drug sbrags ma gsum gyi rjes gnang bstsal /
tshes gsum nas lam rim mchan bzhi ma'i bshad lung gi dbu btsugs nas tshes bcu tham pa'i bar bton kyang skyabs rje gong ma rje bskal bzang thub bstan dbang phyug de nyid kyis /
rje dus gsum sangs rgyas 'gro ba'i mgon / /
pha bla ma'i zhabs la phyag byas nas / /
'khos med kyi ban rgan snyoms las pas / /
dus de ring skyo ba'i glu chung len / /
spyir sangs rgyas bstan pa rin po che / /
phyogs kun tu nam langs skar ma 'dra / /
sgos kun mkhyen bla ma'i gdan sa 'dir / /
dus deng sang khrom las ngo sor khyer / /
rje sangs rgyas kun dngos bla ma de / /
gnas mi mngon zhi ba'i dbyings su gshegs / /
bstan 'dzin du rlom pa'i bla chen 'ga' / /
'thab rtsod dang 'khrugs slong las kyis brel / /
tshul mthun kyi skyes bu dam pa rnams / /
thugs khrel gyi ngang du zhum zhing bzhugs / /
lung rigs kyi dbyangs sgrog phal cher yang / /
phyogs lhung gi gtam gyi gad rgyang sgrog /
btsun gzugs kyi bstan bshig 'ga' re ni / /
ngan las kyi mgo 'phang re zhig mtho / /
ltas ngan gyi 'byung bya rgyab ser 'gas / /
mun nag la skyabs byas than skad sgrog /
lung las kyi mtho ba'i chos rgyal de / /
mi mang gi khrod du dma' 'beb gleng / /
sha med spu med kyi khwa ta 'gas / /
ngan skyug gi khrod na dga' bzhin 'gying / /
snga phyi yi mtha' 'obs ma mthong ba'i / /
re zhig gi rta rgyug spro na yang / /
bka' chad kyi g.yang la lhung ba yis / /
dar rgud kyi ltad mo mthong yang srid / /
kun mkhyen gyi thugs bskyed ma zad na / /
mchod yon gyi nyi zla zung 'brel gyis / /
nag phyogs kyi mun pa rab bcom nas / /
bde skyid kyi pad tshal cis mi bzhad / /
ces shing yos zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes bdun la 'brog stong nas 'khyag sgang la gcig pur skyo glu blangs zhes phebs /
khyad par shing yos lo'i dbyar ngor srid skyond dpa mang rin po che la phyag yig gnang par /
phrag dog rlung dmar 'khrugs pa'i rgya mtsho dang / /
dga' sdug snang ba sprin par nyi shar 'dra / /
yid snang char sprin nang 'khyug glog lta bur / /
gyur 'di yang na dam sri'i 'phrul zhig gam / /
min na ngan goms bag chags sad pas lan / /
'di dag 'di phyi'i legs tshogs 'jig pa'i rgyur / /
nye bar dgongs te rkyen sel rim gro dang / /
gtso cher rang sems rta pho gnyen po yis / /
rta kha gyen du bsgyur la ma 'bad na / /
skyag lang shor rang drag na mgo log gi / /
dkon bkra'i dge bshes bla brang phyag mdzod pa / /
'phrin las ming 'dzin ji bzhin 'gyur gyis dogs / /
gtam 'di sha tsha'i snying gtam drang bo dang / /
ma zad rang gzhan skyon mang bya bzhag gis / /
rgyal khams brlag pa'i rgyur song mang mthong nas / /
tshul 'di drang bor smras la yid gtad 'tshal / /
gcig tu deng dus kho bo tsam zhig las / /
nyid la sems gting sha yang tsha ba dkon / /
gnyis su 'jig rten bya ba la mkhas shing / /
nyams myong ldan zhing 'chad mkhan nyin skar tsam / /
de phyir 'di 'dra'i bslab ston byed mkhan zhig /
ma mthong phyir na yin lugs 'di bzhin smras / /
zhes phebs pa'i thog tu bab ste ser gzugs dag gis bsam sbyor log pa 'ba' zhig gis ser dmag bslangs 'ur zing che bar byung ba la bsten nas rje 'di bas lam rim mchan bzhi ma'i bshad lung re zhig mtshams 'jog dgos byung 'dug nyer gcig la slob ma 'ga' zhig gis bskul ngor dbyangs can ma dkar mo thun mong ma yin pa dang /
dmar mo'i rjes gnang bcas bstsal /
mkha' spyod ma'i dbang bzhi byin rlabs yang gnang /
de nas dgon par zing 'khrug gis sos mi bde bar gyur /
gang la rtsod pa yod pa de nas ni / /
dpag tshad brgya yi pha rol 'gro bar bya / /
zhes gsungs pa ltar rje bla ma rin po che 'di nyid kyis zing 'khrug de dag las bshol dgos dgongs nas ri khrod maN+Dal byang chub gling du phyag phebs gnang /
de nas sa skyong dam pa ching wang yum sras la tshe dbang brgya rtsa gnang /
zla ba drug pa'i tshes nyer bdun nyin zi ling nas ma ches sang gi dmag gtos che ba lhags pa'i rkyen gyis maN+Dal ri khrod de nas kyang ma bzhugs par phyir dgon par phebs /
maN+Dal ri khrod rgya dmag gis gtor bsreg byas te lhag med du btsom pa phyis kyang bskyar gso ma thub 'dug maN+Dal ri khrod nas gdan sar phebs pa'i phyi nyin nangs par thu'u bkwan rin po cher mjal /
dus ngan snyigs ma'i byed spyod dar drags pas phan sleb chung yang thugs lhag bsam mdzad pa bka' drin che zhes zhus /
de'i phyi nyin nangs par srid skyong rin po ches rje 'di bar 'bod mi gdan 'dren pa mngags te gnas tshul 'di la ci drag gi bka' 'dri gnang bar rje 'di bas rim gro gtos chen res bzlog 'gro zhes phebs /
yang khong gung thang rin po cher mjal du phyin /
thugs glod pa'i skabs min par dgon ma lag sde dang bcas pa rjes sor yang sprul rin po che'i phyag tu 'byor nges shig shul gnas rnams kyi khur du bab tshul zhus pas /
brtson pa ci lcogs bgyid ces gsung phebs /
snga gong rje 'di bas a mchog rin po cher yang zing cha 'di mi 'ongs pa'i skyabs 'jug nan cher zhus par lan la khong tshos nga'i ngag la mi nyan gzhan ci byed ces gsungs nas thugs 'tshub nyams gnang /
rje 'di bas 'o na ci byed zhus pas 'ong rgyu red thabs kyang zad ces gsungs pa rje 'di bas thugs la yod gshis khong da ni sdod pa'i dus min 'gro dgongs nas mtsho khar phebs te sos bder spang ljongs nas lam rim bsdus don gyi 'grel ba de gsung rtsom gnang /
de nas cher ma 'gyang par bde 'jags byung ba'i yi ge bden min rdzun min zhig 'byor bas khong phyir dgon par phebs /
thugs brtson cher mdzad de dkon mchog la gsol 'debs chos skyong la 'phrin bcol gnang /
khong gi thugs la skyabs mgon yab sras kyi thugs rjes mi skyon snyam pa shar gsungs /
de skabs khong gi mnal lam du khro bo sngon po zhal dbyibs ches mi mdzes pa zhig gis sna drangs te 'bag gyon pa ches mang bo zhig gis /
yab sras brgyud par bcas pa'i thugs rje dang / /
byin rlabs nus mthu bsam gyis mi khyab pas / /
zhes 'don bzhin par 'cham byed kyang khong gis mjug grub kyi bar du gsung bzhin 'gro ba rmis pas mnal sad pa dang kun mkhyen yab sras kyi thugs rjer nges 'drongs byung bas blo bde gsungs shing /
de nas khong gis /
rigs gsum sgyu 'phrul blo bzang grags pa dang / /
'jam dbyangs bzhad pa'i sku tshe 'phreng brgyud kyi / /
rmad byung thugs bskyed bden pa'i mthu byin gyis / /
nag phyogs gdug pa'i bsam sbyor zhi bar mdzod / /
ces bka' rtsom mdzad de slob ma mang bo zhig la lung gnang /
bla slob tshang mas bka' rtsom de gsung bzhin du mtha' bar phebs nas rgya hos dpon po thong si ngo mar zer bar gus tshul gyis nged cag grwa ba thams cad dpon su yin gyi mnga' 'og gi chos 'don mkhan yin pas dgon pa grwa tshang dang bcas par gnod mi byed par khyed kyis shes zhes zhus par /
dpon des mthe bong bstan te bla ma zer ba khyod red zer zhing bdu khang gtor byed kyi me sgyogs btsugs yod pa sogs bsdus nas dgon pa la skyon mi gtong bar byas /
nang chen re gnyis dang maN+Dal ri khrod ma ches tshang gi dmag gis gtor bshig btang ba las dgon byings la gnod pa ma byung ba yang rje 'di ba'i byin rlabs dang thugs rje thabs mkhas kho na'i drin yin no / /
khong gi zhal nas sngar chung ngu'i dus chos skyong khog zhugs kyi lung bstan zhig la /
phrag dog gya gyu'i dri bzhon 'tshub ma nas / /
zhe sdang du ba'i rgyal mtshan 'dzin pa yis / /
gti mug gnyis 'thung bskyon pa'i na ba ste / /
nga rgya ri bo 'bigs byed drag tu 'bebs / /
zhes pa thog tu bab kyang kun mkhyen yab sras kyi thugs bskyed kyis gtso bor dgon 'di gra ma chag pa zhig byung bas nyin mtshan kun tu sems la bcang rgyu tshe gcig la go chod pa gcig pur sems yod ces gsungs /
zhal 'phros la skyabs mgon sku phreng dang /
bde thang tshang sku phreng yab sras dad dang dam tshig gtsang stabs skyabs mgon mchog gi rnam thar mjug rdzogs par grub yod pas lung gi thog ma gsan na legs zhes gsungs pa bzhin bde thang sprul ba'i skus lha dar che legs bcas snyan gsan phul bas thugs dgyes tshor dang bcas rje nyid kyis mdzad pa'i skyabs mgon bskal bzang thub bstan dbang phyug gi rnam thar kha skong rin po che'i 'phreng ba'i mdzes rgyan lung gsung bshad ngo mtshar ba du ma dang bcas nyin gcig la bstsal /
'di skabs bde thang sprul ba'i skus mtshan lam du skyabs mgon rin po che'i mdun du 'jal te bka' chos la snyan gsan phul /
khong nas rje rin po che'i rnam thar gnang gi yod pa zhig rmis 'dug 'di yang rje 'di ba skyabs mgon thams cad mkhyen pa dang thugs rgyud gcig par ma zad skyabs mgon mchog kyang rje rin po che dang thugs gcig pa'i mtshan ma yang dag go / /
ma ches tshang gi 'khrug zing mu mthud byung bar brten sos bde bar sdod pa'i skabs ma byung bas hor gtsang dgon gsar du phebs /
de nas 'jigs byed zhe dgu ma /
dgra nag lha bcu gsum ma /
gshed dmar lha bcu gsum ma rnams la las rung gi bsnyen pa btang /
lo mjug bde thang sprul ba'i skur phyag yig gnang bar /
lo snga phyi 'di dag tu dgon 'dir gegs cha shin tu che bas skyabs mgon mchog gi yang sprul dang bstan pa'i 'phel rgyas kyi ched du chos rgyal gyi bsnyen pa gnad smin zhig mdzad na legs tshul kyang phebs /
hor zla bcu ba'i tshes nas bdud ris kyi phyogs kun nas reb kong phyogs kyi rong 'brog gi dmag gtos chen rgyab rten du g.yar te bkra shis 'khyil 'di ming brda rjes shul tsam yang med par byed rtsis byas kyang mchog gsum gyi byin rlabs dang srung ma'i 'phrin las kyis kho tsho'i bsam pa dang go bzlog te reb kong ba rnams rgyas pham /
ma ches tshang gis dmag dpung btegs te a mchog gi steng du phyin /
bla brang ngos gtsang du lus stabs khong rin po che 'di ba phyir rang dgon du phebs nas bla slob tshang ma zhal 'dzoms te gnam lo gsar bzhad kyi dga' ston myong rgyu byung /
'di skabs mnal lam du brag dmar ker langs 'jigs su rung ba zhig yod pa'i rtsar rnga rol dang bcas bag tse'i gsol kha zhig btang /
gshis phyin 'gro 'dod pa yin tshe 'gro zhes skyabs mgon gong ma de nyid ga shed gshegs rjes su phebs pas phyogs kun brag ri sngo sangs ngos mnyam pa sgo khyim lag mgo shong tsam pa la phebs pa'i rjes mi zin pa zhig byung ba rmis pas dgon gsar der ma bsdad par phyir dgon steng du 'ong pa yin zhes gsungs /
'di yang skyabs mgon mchog gis rje 'di ba la dgon 'dir bzhugs rgyu las gzhan du ma phebs gsungs pa bzhin rje 'di ba dgon 'dir mi bzhugs tshe dgon par gegs cha che bas skyabs mgon mchog gis dgon 'dir gdan drangs par mngon no / /
dgung grangs nga bzhi ba rab tshes sa mo lug gi lo'i zla ba dang bo'i tshes lngar grub rgyal lugs kyi tshe dbang /
sgra mi snyan gyi tshe dbang /

dwags po'i gsang 'dus kyi bskyed rdzogs /
'jigs byed bskyed rim dngos grub snye ma /
paN chen chos rgyan gyi bde mchog bskyed rim /
de'i gsung lta khrid dran pa bzhi ldan /
sku bar ba'i yi dam sgrub skor sogs lung mang bo gnang /
lo ltar sa ga'i bco lnga'i nyin grwa tshang bzhis lhan cig tu bzang spyod stong gsum bsgrub rgyu'i thebs su dngul srang nyis brgya dang bdun cu tham pas sbyor 'jags mdzad /
lo re bzhin mgon po'i zhi rgyas kyi gtor sgrub res mos tshugs pa'i gtong thebs su dngul srang brgya dang lnga bcu bzhag zhabs brtan lha khang du dge 'dun zhal grangs so gsum gyis smyung gnas mdzad pa'i thebs su dngul srang brgya dang nyi shu tham pa sbyor 'jags mdzad de smyung gnas kyi rgyun btsugs /
sman pa grwa tshang la thub pa dam tshig gsum bkod kyi bdag 'jug nyin bdun gyi mchod thebs su dngul srang brgya dang bco lnga sbyor 'jags mdzad /
cho ga chog rkyang btsugs te phag lo nas bdag 'jug 'dzugs rgyu'i gsungs bkod dang de yang zhogs khar sman chog yid bzhin dbang rgyal dang /
gung tshigs dang dgung ja la bdag mdun dbang chog bcas rdzogs par byed dgos pa'i gsung bkod dang /
rdo rje 'dzin pa'i dkyil chog la kha skong gi tshul du cho ga cha lag yongs su rdzogs pa tshang ba'i lhan thabs kyang gsar rtsom mdzad /
'du khang chen mo'i steng thog rnams ma grub par yod pas de'i ched du dngul rdo tshad gsum gnang /
sman pa'i 'du khang gsar bskrun gyi sar lto 'phye'i thig dang /
brtag bslang sbyang gsum gyi bkod khyab dang /
bde thang rdo rnams pa lag gi blar bskos te rdo btegs pa'i mtha' las byung ba'i rung khang gcod pa sogs lag len mtha' dag 'dul ba dang mthun par byed dgos kyi gsung bkod zhib rgyas gnang nas zla ba lnga ba'i bco lnga la gdan sa bkra shis 'khyil phyogs su chibs kha bsgyur /
gdan sar phebs te bstan 'gyur lung rgyun gang yod yongs rdzogs kyi lung /
bde gsang 'jigs gsum gyi dbang /
mi 'khrugs pa lha bcu gsum gyi dbang /
bde mchog rab 'byams kyi nang tshan phag mo skor gyi dbang gsum /
dus 'khor spyi bka'i dbang sta gon dang bcas pa /
bla ma byams pa rin po che'i gsung skor 'ga' zhig gi lung sogs dang /
bde thang sprul skus zhus ngor mkhas grub sangs rgyas ye shes kyi gsung 'bum gyi lung /
rje nyid kyi gsung gi skor las sgo mang rin po che'i rnam thar dad pa'i khri shing rgyas pa'i me tog bde thang rin po che'i rtogs brjod /
dril bu lus dkyil gyi bdag 'jug 'jigs byed dbang bshad /
bzang spyod 'bru 'grel /
rigs gsum sgyu 'phrul sogs kyi sho lo ka rnams kyi lung gnang /
bde thang mkhan sprul la dpe 'dzin skyor sbyang dpe ltas dpe khrid /
lung rigs kyi dgos gcod sogs dang /
bka' chos nyan rgyu /
mtshams bsnyen sgrub gang thad nas brtson pa rgyun chags dgos tshul dang /
khong rang nyid kyang dgung lo nga bzhi tsam la slebs song bas khom pa mi 'dug ces bslab bya gnad smin dang /
gsung dgongs gzhi can 'ga' zhig gsungs /
sgo mang rin po ches mdzad pa'i bsnyen sgrub sbrags ma'i 'don sgrig dang /
brag dkar bka' bcu'i bcu cha'i sbyin sreg tshe dbang 'chi med rdo rje'i srog shing /
rdo rje 'dzin pa dkon mchog rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i lam rim tshigs bcad ma sogs kyi lung gnang /
dgu 'cham steng hor gtsang du phebs nas zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes nyi shu'i bar sku mtshams mdzad /
'di skabs bka' 'gyur bstan 'gyur gnyis gdan 'dren mdzad /
gdan sar phebs nas 'di ga'i grwa ja'i tshogs zangs 'ga' zhig gis brgyags rtsed kyis bcag kyang ci mi snyam par lo shas la lus 'dug pa thugs la gzan pas rgya dngul rdo tshad drug gis bsgrubs te zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i tshes bco lnga la sbyor 'jags mdzad /
dgung grangs nga lnga ba rab tshes lcags pho sprel lo la smon lam nang du thu'u bkwan rin po che'i gsung gi mkha' spyod chos skor gnang /
tshes bcu bdun nas bde thang sprul skus zhus ngor kun mkhyen gong ma'i gsung 'bum gyi lung gnang /
zla ba gsum pa'i tshes brgyad nas phyag mdzod mkhan po sprul ba'i skus zhus ngor byang chub lam gyi rim pa'i dmar khrid thams cad mkhyen par bgrod pa'i bde lam gyi khrid smin rgyas su gnang ste mchod pa rgya chen po dang bcas 'bum ston jo bo'i mdun nas sems bskyed mchod pa gnang /
'di skabs khrid nyan pa bo rnams la thams cad kyis lam rim chen mo'i sa bcad dam min kyang bde lam gyi sa bcad yod par gyis la lam rim shar sgom lta bu re gal che tshul sogs kyi bka' gnang /
zla ba gsum pa'i nyer lnga'i nyin sgo mang mkhan sprul /
bde thang mkhan sprul /
legs tshogs dang gsum la kun mkhyen gong ma'i gsung 'bum gyi khrod nas bka' rgya ma'i skor gnang ste mjug tu nged kyi bka' chos kyi phyed sgo mang tshang dang phyed ba de thang tshang ste khyed rnam gnyis kyi phyag na yod gsungs /
de nas ma 'gyang bar sku bsnyun gyi rnam pa mdzad /
slob ma so so dang grwa tshang so so nas zhabs brtan phon cher bsgrubs /
brtan bzhugs kyang phul na'ang dwangs skyed cher ma byung /
nyin zhig zhal nas gdung mdun du song nas mchod me dang snyan shal re phul la skyabs 'jug zhu dgos /
de yang nged ma shi bar yun ring bor bsdad na spyir bstan 'gro'i don dang khyad par kun mkhyen 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa yab sras kyi thugs bskyed smon lam gyis bzung ba'i dgon pa grwa tshang dang bcas pa la phan thogs pa zhig yin na myur du nad 'di las grol rgyu'i skyabs 'jug dang de min phan pa gang yang med na sdug bsngal mi myong bar myur du 'chi ba'i skyabs 'jug zhus /
bcos bsgyur mi byed par 'di bzhin gyis zhes phebs pa bzhin bsgrubs pas phyi'i nangs par nas rim bzhin dwangs /
'di yang rnam thar ya mtshan pa'o / /
'di skabs shig tu gung thang blo gros zhes pa'i bshes gnyen mtshan yongs su grags pa des kyang thugs ma bde bar kha dar zhig bskur te zhal 'don gyi skabs sogs su khyed rang gi sku tshe brtan pa'i ched du dmigs na legs tshul gsungs pa bzhin snyan bskul zhus par khong gi zhal nas ngas tshe gang bo 'dir kha ton dang dge sbyong gang byas thams cad tshe 'di'i ched du dmigs nas 'don ma myong zhes gsungs shing sku bsnyun lhag med du song /
de nas bde thang sprul skus sngar nas gsol ba btab pa bzhin kun mkhyen 'jigs med dbang bo'i gsung 'bum gyi lung yang bskyar zhus pa'i lan du spyir bka' chos la bar chad shin tu che ba skyabs mgon mchog nas gsungs pa'i sku rim re yod kyang 'don ma thub gsungs pas zhabs rim ci dgos kyang bsgrub zhus par sku rim rnam gsum /
bgegs mthar byed kyi 'phreng sngags dang bdud tshar gcod pa'i sngags sgrubs zhes bka' gnang /
zla ba drug pa'i tshes gsum nas skyabs mgon 'jigs med dbang bo'i gsung 'bum yongs rdzogs dang gzhan yang byang chub bde lam gyi khrid /
sa skya'i gser chos bcu gsum /

mdo sde bskal bzang sogs kyi lung dang /

zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes lnga nas legs bshad snying bo'i bshad lung /
man ngag rin chen spungs pa'i lung bcas bstsal to / /
dgung grangs nga drug pa rab tshes lcags mo bya'i lo'i zla ba dang bo'i nyi shu tham pa nas nyin gnyis la dga' ldan lha brgya ma'i gzhung bsrangs dang chu bcud len sogs kyi khrid zla ba gnyis pa'i tshes drug nas lam rim mchan bzhi ma'i bshad lung /
byang chub bde lam gyi khrid smin rgyas su gnang /
gsum pa'i tshes nas zhwa lu ba'i sprul ba'i skus zhus ngor grub pa'i dbang phyug mi tra dzo ki nas brgyud pa'i dkyil 'khor re drug gi dbang bskur yongs rdzogs sku bzhi'i sa bon thebs nges su bstsal zhing gsung bshad kyang 'byams klas pa gnang /

bcu drug la gong ma gong chen gyi dbang /

bde thang sprul skus zhus ngor gung thang 'jam pa'i dbyangs bstan pa'i sgron me'i gsung 'bum bka' rgya ma dang bcas pa'i lung dgyes bzhin bstsal /

lcags mkhar gyi 'don sgrig dang thig rtsa sogs la gsung bkod zhib gsal dang 'jigs byed bsnyen sgrub sbrags ma'i khrid dang lung yang gnang /
de nas dug kyA dgon par phyag phebs /
der kun rig gi dbang dang gnod sbyin dregs pa lcam sring gi rjes gnang bstsal te bstan 'gro spyi'i zhabs rim du lcam sring gtor sgrub 'dzugs dgos tshul bkod khyab zhib rgyas gnang ba ltar phyis shel dgon gyi bskal bzang rgya mtsho mngags te legs par btsugs /
de nas rim par bgrod de bcu gcig nyin lung ba'i phu nas zhag mal byas te phyi nyin drug pa'i tshes bco lnga'i nangs par lam thog nas sgo mo lha brag dang shel dgon phyogs la mjal bar kha dog sna tshogs pa'i 'ja' tshon du ma dang sprin dkar cher 'khrugs pa'i go bar phyes nas lha brag dang shel dgon phyogs gsal bar gzigs pas de phyogs su phyag 'bul ba sogs mdzad nas phyir gdan sar phebs te gdan sa'i bzhugs spyil du 'byor nas zla ba drug pa'i yar tshes nang tshe gcig nyams len gyi khrid /
kun mkhyen 'jam dpal zhal lung khrid yig steng nas 'jam dpal zhal lung gi khrid gnang /
'khor chen dbang yang bstsal /
zla bdun pa'i tshes bcu nas nyin gsum la lho brag snyan brgyud kyi rjes gnang yongs rdzogs /
nyi shu la sta gon sngon du btang nas rdog dkyil bdun gyi dbang /
sbas don kun gsal gyi bshad lung /
'jigs byed bcu gsum ma'i bskyed rdzogs kyi khrid /

'od dpag med la brten pa'i 'pho khrid /

smon lam drug byams smon /
yon tan gzhir gyur ma sogs kyi lung bstsal /
khong gi zhal nas rgyang ring nas pha gzhis mthong ba na ka bzhi gdung brgyad kyi rjes su song 'dug pas yid pham zhes gsungs shing ngag dbang bkra shis tshang dang mnyam du skyo ba skyes pa'i zhal 'phros mang bo gnang zhing mthar khong gis gros mgo bton te 'khrungs gzhis kyi shul du mchod rten rmang gzhi 'dom phyed dang brgyad yod pa bzhengs /

rab gnas gyi skabs mkha' la sprin dkar ling ling mang bo dkrigs pa'i bar du 'ja' tshon gyis sprel ba sogs ltas ngo mtshar ba mthong skabs mang mang gi dga' dad ches cher rgyas /
de nas bis mdo dgon du phyag phebs /

gur mgon khang du de ka'i mgon khang ba rnams kyis zhus ngor mgon khang nang nas dpal ldan gur gyi mgon po khro bcu'i bskor ba'i rjes gnang dang rgyal ba bsod nams rgya mtsho'i gsung gi gur gyi gtor chog khong rang nyid kyi gsung gi gur gyi 'phrin bcol dang gsol 'debs mtshan sngags dang bcas pa'i lung bstsal /

de skabs khong gis gsungs pa /
yid gting nas 'khul ba zhig byung bas bcom ldan 'das dpal 'khor lo sdom pa yab yum la gdung ba'i yus kyis gsol ba 'debs pa'i mgur dbyangs shig gsar spel byas zhes gsungs /

a rol sprul ba'i sku rin po ches gtsos reb kong ri khrod pa spyi'i zhus ngor sngags rim chen mo'i bshad lung gnang /
sngar nas yang yang gsol ba btab kyang zhal nas reb kong phyogs shig nas stabs 'grig yong zhes gsungs pa bzhin 'di skabs thugs dgyes bzhin rngog dkyil bdun gyi dbang yongs rdzogs sta gon bcas gnang zhing sngar dus 'khor dbang gi skabs lhag gnas byas pa'i rdor dril kyang bstsal /
shel dgon spyi'i zhus ngor bzhi ba'i mar ngo'i tshes bcur rnal 'byor ma rgyud kyi rtse mo bcom ldan 'das dpal 'khor lo sdom pa bde mchog lha re gnyis can gyi dbang bskur te mjug tu tshogs skabs gnas ri'i rtse mor 'ja' tshon shar ba dang tshogs gtor skabs gnas ri'i rtse mor 'ja' tshon shar ba dang tshogs gtor las bdud rtsi bab pa sogs legs pa'i ltas dang mtshan ma mang bo byung /
tshogs phud gnas khang du bskyal /

de nas se chang dgon du phebs /

slar dkyil 'khor dgon du phyag 'byor byung ste 'grel ba bzhi sbrags kyi dbu nas chos thun gcig gnang ste chos grwa gsar bar zhal gso gnang nas slar rang dgon du phebs te kun mkhyen gsung 'bum gyi lung dang dbu ma'i dgag bya ngos 'dzin gyi bshad lung sogs gnang /

phyag rdor gtum chen gyi rjes gnang /
stag tshang lha mo tshul khrims zhes pa'i bkra shis 'khyil gyi dge bshes grags can des zhus ngor thu'u bkwan gsung mkha' spyod chos sbyor dang mkha' spyod be'u bum gyi lung /
bka' 'gyur gyi dbu btsugs te mdo sde bskal bzang dang rgya cher rol ba'i lung bstsal /
sngon chad rab byung bco lnga ba'i shing byi lor paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa sku phreng dgu ba blo bzang thub bstan chos kyi nyi ma dge legs rnam rgyal dpal bzang bo rgya nag tu chibs bskyod skabs bla ma rin po che 'di nyid kyi zhal snga las bka' chos 'ga' gsan bzhed kyis lan gru nas gdan 'dren gyi bka' shog gnang byung yang bla ma rin po che 'di bas dus rtag tu khengs skyungs gnang stabs cha gang thad nas bdag de lta bu'i 'os su mi 'dug gsungs shing /
khyad par skyabs mgon gong ma rje bskal bzang thub bstan dbang phyug gi gsung las phyogs gzhan du yengs ma lam la phyin pa bas rang dgon 'dir 'chad spel re thub na legs zhes phebs pa thugs la bzhag nas dgongs zhus kyi gsung shog phul nas zhal gyis ma bzhes /
de rjes slar yang sog yul nas gsung shog 'byor bar skyabs mgon bskal bzang thub bstan dbang phyug gi gsung de dgongs pa gzhan du bkral te dbang khrid gang dgos kyi tho dang bcas bka' lung rgya can tsha nan che ba phebs /
'di'i skabs kyi phan tshun gnang ba'i chab shog snga phyi dag ni bla ma rin po che 'di nyid kyi gsung 'bum khrod kyi chab shog skor du bzhugs 'dug paN chen rin po che sku 'bum du phebs nas yang gdan 'dren pa slebs te khal rta'i 'u lag tshun chad bsgrig bkod kyis gsung 'phrin bcas bstsal bas sku 'bum du phebs dgos byung /
lo de'i zla ba drug pa'i nyi shu drug gi nyin gdan sa nas sku btegs te zla bdun pa'i tshes gcig la zhong shan du 'byor /
der zhong shan lha chen la bzang gos yug gnyis las grub pa'i snam sbyar khyad 'phags /

pan chen mchog gi zhal nas bka' chos zhu dgos kyi skor 'di tsho yin /

paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa zla ba bdun pa'i nyi shu'i nyin char chu dang 'dam gyis lam mer gyis gang ba'i nang du bka' chos thugs bzhed che ba'i dbang gis gshed du 'jam dbyangs sgar bar phyag phebs gnang ste bka' chos zhus pa la mgon po'i be'u bum gyi dbu btsugs te yongs rdzogs dpe ris dang bcas pa gnang /
de rjes paN chen mchog nas thugs khom skabs nam yod du zhal bzhi ba'i be'u bum phyi ma bcas gsan bzhes mdzad /
paN chen mchog gi zhal nas nga rang rgya yul sogs phyogs med 'grims pas grib kyis gnod pa ches shin tu che bas rdo rje rnam 'joms kyi bum sgrub byabs khrus dgos tshul phebs gnang bzhin zhus shing tshe sgrub kyang phul /
zhes gsungs /
bka' chos gsan bzhes kyi skabs shig mdo smad lho rgyud du go gung 'khrug pa'i gtam 'ur ba la brtag pa dgos tshul phebs par brtag pa gnang ste rim gro'ang kha shas phab /
paN chen mchog gis lha mo'i drag po'i gtor chen dgos gsung gnang bzhin khong gis rtse'i mgon khang ba kha shas bcas gtor chen kyang bsgrubs /
yang paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa'i zhal nas /
yar lam tshor yang gtor chen 'di yang bskyar sgrub dgos par shar bas lag len ngos po zhig dgos gsungs pa bzhin khong gis yan lag lang+ga bri sgrub sogs be'u bum dang bstun lag len yang dag cig kyang gnang /
yang bar mtshams shig mgon po'i srog 'khor gsar ba bstan te gzhung dang mthun min zhib 'jug gnang rogs gsungs byung /
slad nas khong gis srog 'khor gsar bzhengs mdzad de rdzas byug pa /

zla ba dgu ba'i nyer gcig gi mtshan srod 'khor tsam na khong paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa mchog gis dus 'khor slob dpon snyan gsan 'beb tu mngags te nangs par gser gdung mdun nas thams cad mkhyen pas dus 'khor bdag 'jug bzhes rgyu yin pas khyed kyang tshogs gral du phebs rogs gnang zhes phebs byung gsungs /
phyi nyin dgu ba'i nyer gnyis kyi nangs snga bar tsha grub tsam la rtse'i dbu mdzad gdan 'dren du byon /

de skabs gzim dpon chen mo nas khong la khyed kyis mar me 'di la thugs smon nan tan mdzad rogs zhus /

zhes gsungs /
gung thun la maN+Dal gyi skabs paN chen mchog gis kha dar dkar ser 'dom gnyis lhag re dang mar me rkong bu che ba bcas rje 'di ba'i phyag tu gtad nas mchod rten gyi bum pa'i sgor phul la thugs smon mdzod ces gsungs pa ltar rje 'di bas thugs smon rgya chen po gnang /
khong gi zhal nas /
'dug gnas su 'khod nas bsam blo zhig btang bar dus phun sum tshogs pa ston pa bcom ldan 'das lha las bab pa'i dus chen dang /
gnas phun sum tshogs pa rje rgyal ba gnyis pa sku bltams pa'i gnas dang /
rten phun sum tshogs pa rgyal ba seng+ge'i nga ro'i sku brnyan 'bum phrag mang bo bzhugs pa'i gser gyi mchod rten chen por thams cad mkhyen gzigs mchog gis dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i zhal phye ste dbang bskur bzhes pas gsang sngags zab mo'i byin rlabs dang 'brel rlabs chen thugs bskyed smon pa'i rgya mtsho dang gcig tu lad mo tsam yin yang nan tan gyis byed bcug pa rgyal bstan spyi dang khyad par 'jam mgon ring lugs dar rgyas yun ring gi ched yin nges la zhar la mtha' med ngan song gi gting rdo bdag 'khor ba mtha' can du bsgrub pa red snyam dga' dad shin tu rgyas shing nam dran res kyis kyang byung /
bka' drin de nyid stong gsum gser gyis bkang ste phul yang gzhal nus min rang gis kyang bdog pa blos ci lcog gis shugs bskyed /
gser dgon nas phyir byon 'phral lta bur dngos skyes dang bcas nub re bzhin mgon po'i gtor chung re thongs gsungs pa bzhin gtor chung nyer gcig re ma chad par byas zhes gsungs /
'dir smras pa /
mtha' yas gsang gsum rol ba dpag med las / /

zhes bla go rdo rje 'chang zhes yongs su grags pa rje btsun 'jigs med 'phrin las rgya mtsho dpal bzang bo'i rnam par thar ba dad pa'i padmo bzhad pa'i bden gtam nyi ma gzhon nu zhes bya ba las chos sde du mar zhabs bskyod de 'gro ba du ma dbugs dbyung zhing paN chen sku phreng dgu bas kyang zhabs la gtugs shing phan tshun dam chos gsan pa'i sarga ste bcu gsum pa'o / /

de nas khong gi thugs la dgun gyi bar du sku 'bum du lus na dgun lhag pa che bas lam bar du bgrod dka' bar dgongs nas de lugs paN chen mchog la zhus par paN chen mchog nas gser sbyangs kyi 'khor lo zhig phul te bzhugs dang chos zhu rgyu yod ces gsungs /

de'i mtshan mor mtshan lam du rje nyid sku 'bum du bzhugs nas khro bcu'i sbyin sreg cig gnang ba'i mdun du gro'i skar ba'i dpon po yod pa shar gsungs /

de rjes thugs dgyes nyams mdzad nas rnam gnyis kyis gsung 'phros gnang ba shar gsungs /

cha bzhi rnams gsungs te phyir phebs /
